de la dolor de la hainche	The pain in the hip
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain comes to the buttock of the thigh, and it is due to cold and moisture, and the patient has been treated with what we have advised in its division, but the cure does not work, and the disease is old:
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	Therefore, you should cleanse the patient of the large phlegms with stinking pills, or other good and similar pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	Afterwards, make the cautery;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	And the method of the cautery is according to two methods:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	This means 'and this refers to the combination of hot remedies, and fire cautery.'
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	Fire cautery follows several methods, among which one is such:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	You should apply the fire cautery on the buttock region, three triangular cauterizations according to this form, and make them deep and broad, with an area between each cautery equal to the size of two fingers, and let these be olive-shaped;
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Never do you apply the fire cautery in the middle of the buttocks, for which there are four according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you see that it needs treatment, apply the circular fire cautery as we have discussed earlier in the dislocation of the buttocks;
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	But do it in such a manner that the circles contain all the hip, and all the ribs be pierced.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the method used in sciatica, when pain remains in the hip and does not reach to the thigh or leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it reaches up to the thigh and leg, then you should apply two cauterizations or until the patient's pain is relieved, and perform three on top of the ankle, with one slightly towards the left side;
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	either use surgical instruments or apply heat to the ribs where they connect to the hip;
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And if the patient feels that the pain extends to the right or slightly below the knee, then apply cauterization where the patient feels the pain, three points or four at each point of the cauterization referred to as 'points'.
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if necessary, do more of this task;
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if the pain is localized around the knee toward the thigh, apply a cautery with either an incising or circular cauterizer, and ensure strict caution in all your cauterizations so you do not let off steam until the cauterizer burns nerves and major arteries, and you do not cause more harm and constriction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen many who performed cauterization on the ankle near the foot, and it worked until their leg was completely healed, and even the toes as well, causing them to be pierced and corrupted entirely.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After an abdominal treatment from which they died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pains are in two parts together, make a cautery on one and on the other, according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the sage instructed on using a thigh cauterizer, which is as follows: make it like this rod and place its head also as big as a finger's knuckle, or slightly less, with joints in between and from one joint to the other cover an area equivalent to the size of a thumb's knuckle.
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	And let the joints be made in two parts, and they should also resemble knots, and have a well-made iron hook;
et c’est li forme:	And here is its form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	And apply it until it becomes entirely red and emits fumes, and then place it onto the buttock of the diseased part, and rotate it over the healthy side;
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	and once the cautery has been applied and heated, leave it for three days;
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	then apply a poultice of butter, and keep the wound open long enough;
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	after the ointment treatment until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albucasim says that we use very little of this cautery for fear of causing harm to his patients, and few people use it;
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	and nevertheless this is among the better cauteries, which can be tolerated, and it benefits where it applies.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	The medical burn tools are such that you make the instrument intertwining in which descends the edge of the door, and it may be made of skin or iron with one long surface, and at its height have two marks, and have between each the size increase of a thumb;
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and they must be opened both above and below, and join together in this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	After placing the loin of the animal lying on its healthy side, place your hand very close to the hip bone;
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After placing it between the two hot circles which are heated by the fire for one hour to the end, allow the patient to feel the heat and the burn.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	For he finds a similar sensation as if of fire;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	And when the biting is past, lift your hand with the tool and raise the buttocks gently by two fingers, and leave it like this for three days, and apply butter until that which is black from the scalding goes off.
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	And let it be for three days until the putrefaction proceeds;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	This would be the final treatment after wound cleaning as long as it is clean.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain has extended up to the thigh or even to the leg, then you should apply the same tool to the waist in the same manner as you did to the buttocks;
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And this is the way for hot baths, and I have written about it in my treatise on correcting medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take wood ashes and live lime, as much of one as of the other, grind them together, and mix them into a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	if there is a small notch ahead where a razor's tip might be able to fit in.
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	and place another pot well filled with water and add alkali and salt and sweet water, as long as there are two layers of powders on top that you will have well grasped in your hand;
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	and let it be like this until the water turns murky or the water becomes as dense as lead, then take all that liquid, and pour it over salt and alkali in the same way as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And at that point, it will be quite murky and administered in the manner of various medicines' preparations and in other cauterizations.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	For it performs the same work as fire and can be used with other medicines for cauterizing well in the buttocks area like pepper, honey, anacardium and salt with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen tells us of a treatment where some men were cured of the pain in their hip and sciatic vein, and all the joints, and he says that no other treatment was done, and it was cured in one instance when this treatment had been performed. And they bathed themselves as Galen instructs below.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And instructs in this manner that you take finely ground green and dry vitriol, and grind it very thoroughly with a little fat, and apply it on the hip and thigh and leg where the pain is situated, and bandage it;
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	And leave it for three hours, ensuring that the afflicted area no longer feels the burn.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then make them enter or bathe until their body becomes slightly warm, and have them rest in bed. The pain will disappear completely and they will be cured.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use such medicine cauteries, if this isn't after the removal of pus.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dioscorides states that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with the fat of a goat, if help must;
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And the cautery should be made in this manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take animal dung and mix it with old oil, and apply this mixture to the hollow located between the thumb at the ankle and the other one called the sole.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	After taking dried goat fat, and place it on the fire until it turns to charcoal, then lay it on the wool, and leave it until it becomes sooty.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	And repeat this process again, and keep doing it in this way until you believe by logic that it will reach the hip, and that the pain subsides.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	And this method of cautery is called "sheep cautery".
de la dolor dou dos	of the pain of the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether by impact or percussion or from too much evacuation, or due to similarity of cold substance spreaded, none of these appearances warrants cauterization, because that which comes from the infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	After that, when the patient has been rid of rotten pills or similar substances, and when it's positioned on its back, at the spot where pain persists, mark three lines diagonally, and in each line perform V cautery sessions or more according to the effectiveness and quantity that the patient can endure.
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	and let the cauteries be done with the type of cautery called "points";
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	and if you see fit, perform three or four point cauteries halfway along the median clavicle according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	This disease often affects young children, and the initial symptoms are that they feel faint when they stand up, and fear;
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	and you find in the last spinal nerve of the back and in us the manifestation that appears on other nerves.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and observe it being treated, if you apply the fire cautery according to this shape.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	So that the cautery pricks every part of the spine equally.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see it, cauterize along the spine with the cautery touching two or three lines, and make the points close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After the cure as long as it is clean according to what we have said, and beware that you do not apply the cautery on blisters which are in the vicinity of a nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	Of the pain in joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When joint pains are due to moistness that spreads through every limb of the body, and when pain comes in the feet, which they call 'gout' properly, and when it is caused by cold, these conditions cannot be cured with medicines alone; instead, treatments involving cautery should be used in this manner:

Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there is need that you touch on the face at the foot, if it makes you cauterize across the whole cautery saying "point" when done.
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains extend up to the knees and other joints, which happens many times, apply the cautery on each knee three or four times for each part, with all parts treated using olive oil;
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you need to do more, do it further, but don't let your hand be off until the pain's expected heat is cooked.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend to the knees and back, one administers the cautery as we have said in our chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if pains occur at the hands, do points inside the second faint lines;
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	And if there remains any pain in the arms, make points on each joint and on the back of the hand;
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pains come up to elbows or up to shoulders, cauterize each part, and give good care to the patient and apply medications.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	And if you treat him well and cleanse phlegm, he will recover with the help of God.
de la routure dou syfac	from the rupture of urine
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When rupture occurs in the intestines, and the bowels descend to the kidneys; this is new, so it's important that when you are curing his eyesight, you don't let him fast on that day.

tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	As long as it is white and excretes gallstones.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Then pull out the boils at their base;

et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	And work the thighs well with the patient, and place one of the servants on his thighs, and another above his buttocks where he shaves the hands;
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	Then place the cautery on the mark at your full hand span, and hold it straight until you touch the bone. If you don't reach it on the first attempt, try again several times until you touch the bone.
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	and remember that the boil should not escape when you use the cautery;
que tu ne le brulasses;	so do not burn it;
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and so that the disease does not die or any other illness occurs.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you do not reach the bone with the cautery, your procedures are worthless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	And it is necessary that the application of the cautery to children be subtle according to their size, and for adults as well, according to their size;
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	after three days, cure the wound with butter until the scab is removed;
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	After applying other ointments until he heals, and let the patient lie on his back for forty days so that the wound is well sealed.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And it is necessary that his exercises be prolonged for some time, so that the sweat does not appear when he wishes to go into rooms.

et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	And let him have good rest, work little and guard against excessive drinking and eating, and avoid shouting too loudly;

de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the abdomen

de dolor anciene en aucun membre	from old pain in no limb

de meselerie	In mixture

Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After the treatment, wash the wound with flour mixed with honey and other treatments until it is healed.

de albaras	From woad

li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment for the sore by cautery

li cure dou feu par fer	The treatment with a fire cautery using a iron

des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of hernias that come to stones

C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	This means fire cautery and water hot cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	Fire cautery is as if you heat the metal of the cautery like a feather from a rooster, and it should be made of well-cast iron to fit over all parts, and there should be delicate margins;

li cure dou trembler	he treats through trembling

des pustules puans	pus-sores
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	Once visible from outside the body bathed, or pus-filled blisters, that come from large decaying matter.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	It is necessary at the beginning when they appear that one performs a cautery on each head of the pustule:
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	A fine fire stick cautery, whose points are taken by the flame, or a long root of sainfoin, or to the lentil-shaped cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And once they are cauterized at the beginning when they appear, according to this manner, and it cannot grow pus ahead, but they get rid of the excess from which they come, and they become healthy;
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	But it must be done after the blood has been evacuated.
quant li artere est copee	When the artery has been cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	Many times great bleeding from the artery that is cut at the wound comes outwards or from incising an abscess, or from the cautery on the limb, and similar things would occur;
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	And there's much inconvenience in stench.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And yet, when this happens to none, if you quickly place your index finger on the wound of the vein, and hold it for as long as the pulse subsides under your finger, and no more droplet comes out;
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	Then apply several small and large olive oil cauteries to them until they are all red.
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	Then apply me, whether large or small depending on the wound and its location where the artery is located, place the cautery on that vein where you hold your finger, and keep the cautery in place until the pulse has ceased.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement .i. autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it jumps out when you lift your finger from the vein, and the cauteries are off the fire, then take hastily another one of the cauteries that are on the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	And don't stop doing this one after another until the pulse is ceased;
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	And see to it that you do not burn through the nerve which is beneath, and let no harm come upon the patient;
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	And know that when cutting near the artery, it's hard to properly suture even if the artery is large; this isn't done through one of the four methods we've mentioned:
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	or by cautery, or by extraction if it hasn't been treated yet, or by strong sewing with thread, or through medications placed which have the power to prevent blood flow;
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	and so tied and restrained afterward.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Who will administer the reattachment by tightly binding with cloths or by placing burning things on, or other similar actions, if it does not help then it likely won't.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if this happens to anyone and they have neither seen nor medicine at hand, then they should place their thumb on the wound of the vein as we've said, and stretch it well until it's properly sutured over the wound and over the vein;
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	And let it not move but moisten it with cold water often that is very cold until the organ becomes frozen and swollen and remains stiff.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And make inquiries about those who need cauterization and medicines.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	This begins the second book of treatments for amputations
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	As we told you in the first chapter, about all diseases where cauterization with fire or hot medicines is necessary, and we discuss their causes, remedies, instruments, and forms of cauterization.
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	And I have covered that chapter on the shoulder up to the elbow, and I will proceed with this chapter along the same path for what is found more easily for what you want.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And as I begin this one, it is necessary that you understand that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first section about cauteries, which means greater caution must be exercised.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the work of this chapter, there is often bloodletting when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and treating wounds, and extracting arrows, and cutting into stones, and similar things;
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	For there is doubt and fear, and many die as a result.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I urge you that you do not embark on folly.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	And none of the ways of people come to healing.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	If they come from those who are so afflicted by their illness that they die lightly due to the foolishness they find in their disease, and the severity of their suffering;
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	And one should have fear about this.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	And for these I will give you their meaning, and say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	Wait, I am here.
et li maladie est despitouse.	And the illness is resistant.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	It is not right for you to consent to those who come to your door with this manner, but rather invest more in respect than in greed. Do not act foolishly, but wisely about what you are certain of and can take knowledge from;
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	And use prediction and guidance in your treatments for your patients, ensuring their health is transformed.
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	And this will help you gain good reputation, fame, and lasting memory.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Dear child, our lords provide good understanding and righteousness to you, and if you wish to aspire from the holy inspiration of their hand, so be it.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Or I have ordered this chapter out of discussion by chapters, according to what is before or the chapter about the cauteries, which I discussed from the head up until the foot, because you will find it easier that which you need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	from the head full of water
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	Know that this disease often arises when the child is born, and when the mother holds the head of the child too tightly;
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	And it never happens due to any other reason that we know of.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	And I have never seen this disease in anyone other than children, and among all those I have seen, death came quickly;
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	And because of this, it seems to me that dividing the work into partial treatments would be worthwhile.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	And I have seen the child of this, where the shoulder was full of water, and the head swelled each day until it could no longer bear it;
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	And suffered so much from the moisture that he died, and this moisture is assembled around the bone at the elbow, between the muscle and the bone;
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	And the operations were such that when moisture is between the muscle and the bone, and the abscesses are small, you split through the head with a wide crack.
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	And make it as long as two of our lengths, while the moisture goes along.
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	and here is the form of the splint:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai .ij. fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If there is more moisture, and the abscesses are larger, make two cuts in a cross-like manner, according to this shape:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	And if the moisture is around the bone, and you see the signs where the head joints are open from each side, and when you press it with your hand internally, it makes a sharp sound that does not stop:
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	So it is necessary that you split the head along its center into three cracks in this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after making the incision, remove all moisture completely outside.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	After restraining the cuts from powders and oils, and I put wine and oil, and leave it like this until the fifth day;
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	Then release him, and treat the wound with poultices and ointments, and allow the head to heal evenly, and then let the patient eat dry meat from a source of moisture until the limb is strong and healthy.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	And another method of incision is to look at where the opening of the abscess is large, and to assemble water;
car aucune fois est elle devant;	for it never faces forward;
aucune fois derrier;	nor does it face behind;
aucune fois en destre;	nor does it face to the right;
et aucune fois en senestre.	nor does it face to the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	Cut accordingly to the size of the wound or abscess opening, and fill with water, and make a cut according to what you are able.
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	and beware that you do not clip the artery;
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	and let blood flow slightly, so that the patient dies from the diffusion of blood and the evacuation of moisture.
de reume	Of cautery from fire, command the sick person to let the hairs grow long and even; and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les .ij. arteres.	When it comes to any disease which is called "catarrh" in the eyes or at the bottom, and this sickness is old, and the treatment with medicine does not help, then the last resort therapy would be cautery using which one cuts off the two great arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	Therefore, when you see them cut off, the patient must recover beyond their head;
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	After rubbing the wound with a rough cloth until the arteries are visible, then pull out the patient's head to its entire length.
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	Then look where the vein is located, and after the ears where both the eyes are, and they should be returned;
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Then mark the signs of the incision, then cut both with a sharp sword for two parts, until the vein size reaches to the bone, and this should be done through the width of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com .ij. dois au traver.	And if you see it, hold the spatula near the artery and vein above, cut also as two inches through.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein has been severed, make sure to continue cutting upwards outward from there.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	And if the artery does not open to touch it, you should measure the size of the gap in three inches, then cut and proceed until reaching the bone;
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	And what needs to be removed of the blood is six cubic centimeters, and by chance somewhat more or less, depending on how well the patient can endure it, and the filling of the artery;
puis regarde la plaie:	Then look at the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	If there is a bone tip mark of syphilis, cut it off where no vein remains, then incise and remove any pus, stitch up the wound and dress it with ointment until it heals.
de emigrainne	"De emigrainne" translates to "from grain" or possibly referring to a process of sifting or removing grains. Without further context, it's challenging to provide an exact interpretation for this specific phrase within the medieval medical treatise. In general terms, in a medical setting, it could relate to procedures involving the removal of grains (such as pieces of gravel or sand) from bodily tissues or fluids.
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When old age approaches, and severe coughing occurs, due to moisture from tears and heat in the temples and elsewhere in the elderly body, as well as similar things, treatment is done using methods of medical cure and all this does not benefit it. Therefore, one should extract the arteries of the temples and apply a cautery, as we have described.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the way to extract them is that the patient should allow their hair to grow from their temples, and listen for the pulse which appears in the temple, because it opens well through its beat, and responds only in some who are too cold;
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	And if it responds, strangle the neck with some cloths, then rub its head with a rough cloth, and raise it in hot water until the pulse becomes clearly evident;
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	Then take the spatula of which here is the shape:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	Then scrape the skin slightly until you feel the pulse, then pull it upwards with needles, and remove well the webs that are off of each part;
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	And if the pulse is subtle, turn it at the tip of the little finger, then scrape that part according to the quantity of the two shoulders.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it's not cut, neither will escape all without pain.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	And bleed from the sixth century onward, until the third.
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	And if the artery is large, it is necessary that you tie it with two loops of a strong silk thread, to prevent putrefaction from occurring before the healing of the wound and to prevent bleeding.
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	Then cut off the excess that is between the two threads at that same time. And then, if you see fit, apply the copper cautery up to the bone as long as the dislocated shoulders are cut.
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	And this is the skilled work, if the patient does not have fever and they have warm complexion.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	For the cauterizing helps to complete the drying process:
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	Therefore, it is of greater help in drying processes.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	It is necessary for the extraction of arteries; one must fill the area with old cotton and place it under well-made tents.
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when they [the arteries] are released, if one uses dry medicinal substances that create heat and tents until it is healed;
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if you leave the artery without stopping bleeding as you work, if you hurry with the copper by cautery, or you fill the area with vitriol and hold it in your hand so that the bleeding is stopped.
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	And if you do not have that present, place ice on the area as long as the bleeding is frozen, and remove the ice with cold water until the bleeding stops, and hold it in accordance with what is necessary;
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	And when the one who is bleeding and more fragile in extracting an artery is involved, you should apply this cautery to sear the vessel of that cautery by two cuts, but let the cuts be well apart to retain heat for longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the instruments are too tight, they hold less of their heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	And there should be between the two knives about half an inch of space. Then when you mark to join the two ends together, and you place the hot iron until it reaches the bone, and cut open in two places;
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	And let there be distance between the two shoulders, because this cautery does not weld completely from end to end;
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	and it is the shape of the cautery:
des larmes	of tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;	When the tears from the eyes are draining through veins above the testicle region of the head muscle, and no benefit is gained from any medicine applied, and you see the face of the patient turning red, and feel the forehead trembling as if with a heartbeat;
et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	And when they are so wet and moist that the paper hairs fall off, and the papers heat up, being scorched by the tears' heat, this treatment requires effort.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front;	And they named the old one 'healer of bruises', and it is that you make the patient who has this disease grow hairs on their head or forehead, then you cut three equal slits across the forehead according to the length of the forehead.

et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins;	And keep your hand away from the connection of the two jaws, and each wound will have an area equivalent to three inches in length.
et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	And have an absorbent sponge and cloth ready to wipe away the blood, then use a sharp spatula from two parts of which this is made.
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision;	From the incision made above the temple up to the second incision;
et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les II fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	And burn the entire area between the two grooves until you reach the line where it meets the bone, then cut along halfway down the second incision up to the other groove, and then remove that pus-filled part.
si boute en la premiere fendure l’estrument qui est apelez «cultellaire», et est tresbien trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part est souef, ne mie trenchans, et c’est li forme:	If you use a tool in the first incision that is called 'culetter', and it is very sharp on one side, and on the other side is hollow, not sharp, and this shape:
Et met le costeit taillant vers la char aerse au keur, et lou costeit souef vers l’os, et lou boute tant qu’il veigne a la moiene fendure.	And make the cut towards the fatty part of the kidney, and let the knife head face towards the bone, and the blade until it reaches to the middle crack.
Et cope toz les vasselz que dessendent dou chief as eulz tant que l’incision soit continue jusc’a ceu qui apert dou keur, et puis autreteil fai en la moiene fendure jusc’a l’autre defuer;	And cut all the blood vessels that descend from the head until the incision is continuous up to where they open into the skin, and then make another cut halfway down the groove up to the other opening;
et puis estrai dou sanc igalment, et espresse lou leu por le sanc pris;	And remove the blood evenly, and expose the area for the taken blood;
puis met en chescune fendure une tente de viel coton, et met sus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile et en aisil, et garde que apostemes chaus n’i veigne;	Then place a piece of old cotton in each groove, and put damp cloths soaked with vinegar, oil, and garlic over them, making sure no pus remains.
et au tier jor deslie lou liien, et i amenistre grant planteit d’aigue tede, puis lou cure d’oignement basilicon avec oile roset, et d’autres cures dont on cure plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And on the third day, release the wound, and I administer large plantings of water turpentine, then the cure with basil oil and rose oil, and other treatments for wounds, until it heals.
dou reume des eulz	from the pus
Quant a aucun vienent catarre agut acostumeement, et tu vois les eulz tenves et petis, et afoiblir la veue, et les papieres brulees;	When dealing with sudden severe catarrhs that are customary, and you see the eyes becoming weak and small, and weakening of sight, and burned paper;
et li poil chieent, et ou chief en parfont a dolor ague, et li malaides esternue;	And the hair falls out, and one feels pain in the forehead, and the patient sneezes, and the body is affected;

pren II parties de flor de froment, et de colofoine IIII parties, et en fai emplaustre;	Take two parts of wheat flower and four parts of clove, then make them into plaster;
et l’aministre en ces plaies por enjanrer char per tout.	And he administers in these wounds to enhance flesh throughout.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	Regarding ear piercing.

de la char des papieres	From the residue of paper

de la gresle	Regarding ice
Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz;	Many times in the papers, one encounters things that seem to freeze in their form and hardness, and for this reason is called 'granulation', and it is a collection of moisture large on the surface of the paper.
li ovraiges est telz:	The treatments are as follows:
pren warde se li grandine se muet d’une part et d’autre, et c’est legiere chose a savoir;	Take care of the silence of the great bone on both sides, and it is a simple matter to know;
fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope.	Then make it wide, then scrape each part slightly, then take it with forceps, and manipulate.
se tu ne la pues coper sens percier un poc la papiere, si ne grieve rien au malaide;	If you can't scrape without piercing the paper slightly, if it doesn't harm the patient;
et se li fendure est grans, si l’assemble a une costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	And if there's a large crack, you put it together at a seam, and treat until it heals;
et s’elle est petite, si n’i faire point de force, car li oignemens la restoure tantost et enjanre char.	And if it's small, don't use any force, because the ointment heals it quickly and nourishes the flesh.
Et se li grandine est dessendans au dedens de l’oreille vers la partie desus, si enverse la papiere, et estent la grandine a unes pinceures, et la cope et presse d’une part et d’autre;	And if the great bone descends within the ear towards the upper part, you should turn the paper, and put the bone at one of the forceps, and manipulate it from both sides;
et se li papiere est esloignie par l’incision, ce ne grieve rien;	And if the paper is moved by the incision, it causes no harm;
et quant li grandine est copee, si leive l’oil d’aigue salee, et cure le leu de ceu qui enjanre char tant que li malaides soit sanez.	And when the large lump is removed, rinse with clean water and cleanse the area around where the infection was until the patient feels better.
de la graisse des eulz	of the grease of the lumps
Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz;	Exinach is a fat that accumulates on the sheets of papers above it, and this happens more often in children than adults, and causes much discomfort to their eyes, and they have catarrh coming out during mornings, and cannot look at the sunlight because tears rush to their eyes;
et por ceu se couchent il sor lor faices adés, et dorment sus, et sont lor papieres desoz lor sorcilz moistes que li enfleure et li apparance ont covert de l’exinach qui apert en l’oil.	And because of this, they lie on their sides and sleep there, and have the papers under their eyes wet due to the sweat and appearance that turn over from the exinach which opens in the eye.
Et quant tu presses lou leu a tes dois et sent l’exirnach entr’ous.	And when you press your hand onto it and feel the exinach between your fingers.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain;	And the method of treatment is such that patients place their head on your healthy part;

et presse a tes dois d’une part et d’autre, si que li exirnach soit assemblez emmi le cercle;	And press with your thumbs on both sides, so that the discharge is gathered inside the circle;
puis fent em mileu de la moistor au spatumile trenchant une fendure dou large, et ne soit mie plus grans que li plaie c’on fait a la sainie de voinne;	Then make in the middle of the moisture at the spleen, cut a slit that is not much larger than the wound you do for the opening of the vein;
et fent le cuir em parfont tant que tu veignes a l’exirnach;	And stretch the leather all around as far as you can see the discharge;
et em plusors dispositions vient exirnach de la fendure, selonc la forme d’une piece de graisse blainche.	And in various orientations comes discharge from the slit, according to the shape of a piece of white fat.
Estrai la donques a tout une piece de drap charpit entre tes dois au defuer, et torne ta main a destre et a senestre tant qu’il soit espars;	Pull out then take one piece of fine cloth between your thumbs at the back, and turn your hand to the right and left until it disperses;
et garde que tu n’ajoster en la fendure, que tu ne viegnes a tout le spatumile jusc’a l’oil, que tu ne le bleces.	And make sure not to adjust in the slit, don't allow all of the pus up to the eye, don't cause any bleeding.

Et s’il vient au leu aposteme chaut, si lou cure d’emplaustres assouajant tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if it comes to cutting an abscess there, then a plaster treatment is applied until the wound heals.
des poilz des papieres	(of paper hairs)
Quant em papieres naissent poilz ajostez autre que li naturez, et sont enveillit, si nuisent as eulz, et font venir manieres de maladies si com larmes acostumees et mollifications des papieres et albugine, tant que c’est cause de la destruction des eulz;	When hair grows out of its natural place and becomes old, if they harm the eyes, they can bring about diseases such as weeping used to be and paper softenings causing impotence, all leading to the deterioration of vision;
et est li cure selonc IIII manieres:	And then the treatment follows four methods:
ou par cautere ensamble feu, ou par medicine ague selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre de cautere, et est fais ou par incision et costure ou par caines, selonc ceu que je dirai.	or by fire cautery with the assembly of heat, or by medicine in water according to what was discussed previously in the section on cautery methods, and it will be done either through cutting and stitching or through bandages, as I shall explain.
Il covient que tu mettes lou chief dou malaide en ton sain, puis torne la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre;	It is necessary for you to place the head of the eye in its healthy position, then turn the paper towel under your left hand;
s’elle est convertie, c’est boin;	If it has turned, that's good;

The paper should be placed diagonally according to this size.
