Clear out the blood, and dry off the excess threads on both edges of the two cuts in all respects. If you see fit to do this;
et se ce non, si n’en aies cure, puis laisse la costure et les filz jusc’a III jors ou IIII;	And if not doing that troubles you, or if it's not of concern to you, then leave the stitch and the threads until three or four days.
puis cure la plaie sens costure de choses sechans et constrignans, car li papiere se relive au soudement de la plaie et l’assemblement de li, mais li costure est muedre (si com dirent li ancien), et c’est ovraiges sens paor;	Then treat the wound without stitches or bindings. Paper peels off at the healing of the wound and the joining of things together; however, the stitches remain moist (as the old ones say), and this is work without fear.
et si a une autre maniere:	And if there's another way:
et est que tu seignes la papiere d’une figure qui soit ausi com li fuelle de mirte, si com nos avons conteit, a III oncines desevrez selonc la forme qui est ci:	And it is that you seal the paper with a shape that resembles the leaf of myrtle as we have recounted, in three inches cut according to this form:
puis cope ceu qui sormonte as petites forces igalment selonc la forme qui est ci:	Then cut the one that sits above evenly, according to this form:
Et se tu n’as pooir de tenir les tenailles, et li chose n’est mie igalz, si prent une aguille ou il ait I fil, et la boute emmi la figure;	And if you don't have the ability to hold the forceps, and the thing isn't even, take a needle or where there is thread, and hold it in front of your face;
et boute I autre fil delez lou grant larmier, et lou secont fil delez lou petit, et assemble entre tes dois les filz igalment;	and hold the other thread longer than the large artery, and the second thread shorter than the small one, and join the threads evenly between your thumbs;
puis lieve ta main igalment, et lieve tout le cuir sus coi tu as signiet, si com nos avons conteit, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie par costure, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	then lift your hand evenly, and lift all the skin over which you've stitched, just like we have recounted, then join both edges of the wound by suture, and the treatment until it heals;
et se aposteme vient a ton incision, si l’apaise de cerote et de semblans oignement assouajans;	and if an abscess comes to your incision, soothe it with tallow and similar salving substances;
et aucune fois avient que li poil de la papiere sont convertit:	and sometimes the paper hair gets turned inside out:
si covient que tu uses ceu que nos avons dit de l’incision;	If it is necessary for you to use what we have said about incision;
mais li costure en l’une et en l’autre est plus artificialz.	but the stitches in both cases are more artificial.
Li cure des caines si est selonc ceste forme:	The treatment of canines follows this form:
et est que tu convertisses la papiere et la fent dedens selonc ceu que j’ai dit, et puis fai II caines par art, et II liiens subtilz ausi lonc com li papiere et li largesce dou spatumile est;	and you should convert the paper and the cut inward according to what I have said. Then make two canines by art, and also two ligatures as long as the paper is wide, as well as small in diameter equal to the thickness of the bone;
et cope as II chiés de II pars ou tu tiens les filz;	and tie them as two pieces of two parts where you hold the threads;
puis assemble l’un et l’autre subtilment sus ceu que sormonte de la papiere de l’oil, et estrain les II cainnes des II parties forment;	then delicately combine both on top of the paper where the oil is found, and tighten the two canines from each part in a symmetrical manner;
et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, et li cuir qui iert estrainte morra et nercira et porrira, tant qu’il cherra par lui.	And let it like this for a few days, and the skin that is constricted will die, rot and peel off, until it exits through itself.
S’il tarde, si le cope a unes forces, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	If it lingers, if the wound has strength, then he treats it as long as it is clean;
et quant li plaie iert soudee, et si ert levee li papiere, et ne poindront plus li poil;	And when the wound has healed, and if the scab is lifted, and no longer will grow hair;
et c’est li forme des II cainnes que tu feras selonc ceste figure, et selonc ceste quantiteit de lonc et de large:	And this is the form of two hens that you will do according to this image, and according to this length and width:
li ovraiges est telz que tu preignes une aguille subtil, et i boute I fil de soie souef et subtil;	The operations consist in taking a delicate needle, and then you cut off a thread of silk soft and fine;
puis assemble les chiés et noe l’un et l’autre subtilment, et soit li longesce des filz une palme de lonc;	Then join the ends and knot them finely together, and make the length of the threads as long as your palm in width;
puis ordene en la chasse I autre fil subtil de soie briément, et noe les chief dou fil;	Then proceed with this hunt for a finer silk thread, tie it firmly to the end of the thread.
puis mette li malaides son chief en ton sain;	Then place the patient's head onto your healthy side;
et soit delez lou soleil si que li ovraiges soit declairiez, car c’est uns ovraiges subtilz et menus, puis boute l’aguille a tout la chasse en la racine dou poil ajosteit, et la fai percier en la papiere hastanment tant que tu la traies desus lou poil natureil;	And let the sun be over the operation so that all parts are seen clearly, for this is a delicate and small procedure. Then pull the needle out of every hunt into the root of the adjusted hair, and pierce through the paper as quickly as you draw it above the natural hair;
puis estrai le poil jusque sus la chasse, et boute en la chasse celui poil, s’il en i a I ou II ou III ou plusors;	Then pull out the hair up to the tip, and when you find one or two or three or more hairs in it;
puis estrai ta main tant que li poilz veigne fuers a tout la chasse en la papiere avec lou poil natureil.	Then pull your hand until the hairs come out at the tip of the needle with the natural hair.
Et se li chasse est traite et li poilz ne vient fuer avec li, si trairas la chasse au desoz a tout le fil que tu i as ordeneit, tant que li chasse veigne fuer dou pertus desus et que tu la voies par la vision de l’oil;	And if the chase (hunt) is treated and the hair doesn't come out with it, you should pull the hunt to the end of its thread that you have ordered, until the chase feels forced above the wound and you see this through the eye's vision;
adonques si trairas la chasse et le fil, et clo l’oil et lou laisse clo II jors ou III, tant que li poil s’aerde en son leu et naisse li char sus;	Therefore, if you pull the hunt (likely referring to a wound or removed tissue) and the thread, cover the eye and leave it covered for two or three days, until the hair grows back in its place and flesh starts to grow.
et se li poilz est petis, si acompaigne I poil lonc des chevoulz naturez, et soit alevez avec celui ou tu le laisse, tant qu’il soit eslongiez et puis le lieve.	And if the hairs are small, accompany with one hair that is naturally long, and raise it along with whichever you leave, until it becomes extended, then raise it.
de la porriture de l’oil	Regarding eye infections or diseases.
Quant ceste maladie qui est apelee «aleacrati» ou li porriture vient en l’oil, si en i a de II manieres:	When this disease, called "Aleacrati" or the putrefaction affects the eye, if there are two ways:
l’une natureil, et l’autre innatureil.	One natural, and the other unnatural.
Et avient par soudement de plaie, ou de tailleure ou de cautere, et par semblans choses.	And occurs suddenly from wounds, or due to surgeons or cauterization, and through similar incidents.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige en li est que tu fendes celle soudure, et dessevre les levres de li, et met dedens tentes de lin, et la lie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	And the method of opening it is that you cut through that seam, and open the lips of it, and place linen tents inside, and bandage until it's healed;
et ne covient mie que tu uses en la cure de li de choses que sechent et restraignent.	And it is not right to use in treating it with things that dry and restrict.
Car se tu fais ceu, si revient li maladie pire que li premiere;	For if you do this, the illness returns worse than the first one;
mais i oevre de choses amollissans, si com fenugreic;	but use remedies that soften, such as fennel;
et l’arose d’aigue ou altee et semence de lin soient cuites, et oignemens dyaquilon fondut en aucun des oiles, et i envoloupe une tente, et le cure de ceu.	and wash it with hot water or oil and linseed meal that has been cooked, and anoint with garlic melted in any oils, and make a tent, and treat it with this.
Et li tresors de ta cure si est que tu te dones en garde qu’ele ne soude mie selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant;	And the treasures of your treatment are such that you must guard against it not joining together according to its former shape;
et cist ovraiges que nos avons dit nen est fuers que adresemens de ceste maladie, qu’elle ne reviegne selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant.	And these operations that we have described do not leave out directions for this disease, so that it does not return according to its former shape.
de la char qui vient en l’oil	of the fat which comes to the eye
Ceste maladie que est desoz qui vraiement est apelee «axacrati», et est naturelz et accidens.	This disease that is caused by worms is really called "axacrati", and it is natural and accidental.
Li accidens vient de plaie et de fendure et de cautere et de choses semblans;	Accidents come from wounds and cuts, and cauterization and similar things;
et li voie de l’ovraige en li si est que tu preignes un aguille, en coi il ait I fil double, et la fiche en la char, et li fai percier des le senestre larmier tant c’a destre, si que li filz veigne en II chiés de la char;	And the method of performing this operation is that you take an awl in which there is double thread, and insert it into the flesh, and make a cut on the left eyelid as far as the right one, so that the threads go through two layers of the flesh;
puis estent la char au desus a tout l’aguille, et la cope a I spatumile large.	Then there is the flesh above all the awl, and it cuts into the wide spatula-like area.
Et se li figure de la papiere revient selonc ceu qu’il covient, c’est boin;	And if the paper figure returns according to what is required, it's good;
se ceu non, si pren I raseur et le met en la fendure, et torne la papiere, et fent II fendures ou costeit dedens la papiere;	If not, take it easy and place it in the groove, then turn the paper, and make cuts inside the paper;
et soient li chiés des II fendures des II angles de l’incision que tu as copeit, et soit fais uns angles si que quant elles sont assemblees, que li figure soit ausi com li figure d’une lettre qui a non «I griesche»;	And make the two corners of the two cuts corresponding to the two angles of the incision you have made. Ensure that when they are joined together, the figure resembles the shape of a letter 'Y' or 'Griesche';
puis oste celle char, selonc la quantiteit que ses costez est agus desoz, de ceu qui enseut la papiere, puis ajoste les II parties desevrees, et les cout d’un fil de lainne;	Then position that flesh according to the size of its circumference and thickness as indicated by the paper, then adjust the two required parts, sewing them with thread like wool.
puis lou cure de ceu que nos avons dit des medicines mollifians, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then follow the cure as we have described for softening medicines and baths until they are healed.
Et se li maladie vient de fendure ou de costure ou de cautere, si covient que tu fendes une fendure plainne desoz les poilz des papieres, et selonc ceu qui est ci devant;	And if the disease originates from a cut or suture or cautery, it is necessary that you make an incision filled with the hair of papers, and according to what was previously mentioned;
puis desevre entre les II leivres d’une tente, si com j’ai dit;	then cut between the two sides of a tent, as I have said;
et doit on faire l’ovraige selonc la forme de la maladie, car elle est mout diverse en forme, et li saiges maistres appareille engien de tout som pooir coment il faice revenir la figure a sa forme natureil;	and one must do the work according to the shape of the disease, for she is very varied in form, and the skilled masters equip themselves with all kinds so they know how to return the shape to its natural form;
et li malaides meisme, selonc ceu qu’il i covient d’ovraige et d’estrumens em plusors dispositions.	and the patients themselves, according to what requires treatment and instruments in various positions.
dou soudement de la papiere	suddenly of the paper
Quant ceste soudure avient a mains homes en teil maniere que li papiere desus est sodee avec le blanc de l’oil, et ne puet movoir ne faire ses ovraiges naturez, si covient donques que tu i boutes la pointe d’un raseur desoz la papiere, et la lieve en haut;	When this seam occurs between two people in such a way that the paper above is glued with the white of the egg and cannot move or do its natural tasks, then it is necessary to thus insert the tip of a razor underneath the paper, and lift it up;
et l’estent as pinceures, tant que tu copes ceu qui est aert au spatumile subtil, qui ne soit mie trop agus ne trop trenchans, si que li malaides ne puisse soffrir que li spatumile trop agus ne blecent l’oil;	And in the incisions, until you have this one who is in pain under the delicate pus point, which should not be too sharp and not too piercingly dull, so that the patient does not suffer from too sharp pus points and they do not irritate the eye.
et soit ton incision, dont tu escorche celle assemblee, legierement, si que li papiere reviegne selonc sa forme natureil;	and make your incisions on that which is assembled, lightly, so that the skin heals according to its natural shape;
et est sanee toute celle assemblee, et font aucune fois en l’oil aigue salee, et le leve d’aigue douce, et de coliere;	and heal that which is assembled entirely, and perform no sharp washing in the eye, but use salty water, and wear a colander.
puis met entre la papiere et l’oil une tente de lin, et met sus l’oil laine moillie en abun d’uef;	then place a linen tent between the skin and the eye, and put wet wool on top of the eye.
et aprés le tier jor use dou coliere et des choses soudans tant qu’il soit sanez.	and after three days, use a colander and other hot things until it is fully healed.
de l’ungle de l’oil	At the eye's nail
Saiches que li ungle est selonc II manieres:	Know that there are two ways regarding the angle:
elle est nervouse et semblans a I dur syfac, et une autre qui n’est mie nervouse, mais est semblans a blainche moistor congelee, que quant on la touche de fer et on la cuide panre as pinceures, si ne puet om;	It is nerve-like and appears somewhat hard like dough, and another that isn't nerve-like but appears white like frozen moisture. If you touch it with iron and treat it by pricking with pins, then it cannot be moved;
et l’une et l’autre semblance encomence devers le grant larmier, et croist poc et poc tant qu’ele cuevre toute la veue et toute la lumiere et le movement de l’oil.	And both of them start near the large tear ducts and grow slowly, until they cover all vision, light and eye movement.
Et li maniere de l’incision si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz;	And the method of incision is such that when the patient's head meets their healthy state, then they open the eyes;
et lieve la papiere a ta main, puis coil l’ungle as pinceures de petite doubleure, et l’estent au desus;	and lift the paper with your hand, then curl the nail with small pins, and extend it upwards;
puis pren une aguille, et i met I poil de cheval, ou de vaiche, ou de buef, et I fil fort;	Then take a needle, and insert a horse hair, or a cow hair, or a bull hair, and a strong thread;
et double la pointe de l’aguille un poc et la fiche emmi l’ungle, et la perce a tout l’aguille, et lie l’ungle d’un fil et l’estent au desus, et escorche a tout lou poil le costeit de l’ungle qui enseut la prunele et la soie au poil jusc’au chief, puis cope lou remanant en la racine dou larmier a tout lou spatumile subtil et as petites forces, et laisse la char natureil ou larmier, si que par l’incision ne veigne li cors des larmes acostumeement;	and double the needle's point slightly and place it in the nail bed, then pierce through with all the needle, and bind the nail with a thread and stretch it above, and scorch all the hair at the edge of the nail which is adjacent to the cuticle and the tenderness of the hair up to the tip, then cut off the rest from the root near the hinge on all delicate areas and minor forces, and leave nature's sap if necessary, so that by incision there does not flow the body's tears habitually;
et aucune fois s’estent li ungle a l’oncine soulement, et au fil, si com nos avons dit;	And always stretch only the nail to the nail bed and with thread, as we have said;
puis l’escorche on a tout le spatumile souef de coi ci est li forme:	Then for the scorched one, all the hairless skin around which is of this form:
Et garde que li spatumile ne touche la toile charnue et la rompe, et que li prunele ne soit percie;	And see to it that the hair doesn't touch the fleshy lining and tear it, and that the nose tip doesn't pierce;
et aprés l’incision giete en l’oil un poc de seil broiet, et dou coliere fait de litargire, et le laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	and after the cut pour a little of this ointment into the ear, and make a collar from silver, and leave it until the other day;
puis le cure de ceu qu’il i covient tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the one who needs it as long as they are sound.
Et se li ungle n’est mie nervouse, et tu ne pues bouter l’aguille, et li uncines n’i puet entrer, maintes fois est curee ceste semblance d’ungle de medicines;	And if the nail isn't sensitive and you can't push in the needle, and it doesn't enter under the nails, this condition of the nail is often treated with medicines;
et naissent sicom j’ai conteit en la division, et se tu la vues coper, si oevre l’oil dou malaide, et pren le spatumile legier poc agut selonc ceste forme:	and they grow like I have described in the section of separation, and if you see it cover, work on the eye with the patient, and take the hair carefully slightly sharp according to this form:
Et reis l’ungle desus subtilment, et se tu vois qu’elle amenuise point et li rasion i apresse, si distille de ta bouche en l’oil coliere fait de litargire et dou coliere rouge et seil broiet, et estoupe l’oil jusc’a l’autre jor;	And grasp the nail gently from above, and if you see that it doesn't diminish at all and your reason is quick, then drop a stream from your mouth into the ear canal made of argentum (silver) and red neckring, and apply a paste to the ear until another day;
puis rencomence l’autre ovraige selonc ceste meisme oevre, tant qu’elle soit toute ostee.	Then start the next operation in the same way, until all of it is removed.
Se aucune chose ne t’est contraire en l’oil, si com aposteme chaus, adonques la lait, et cure premier l’aposteme chaut tant qu’il soit sanez, puis rencomence l’ovraige si com devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If there's nothing against your sight, for instance with pus-filled sores, then treat it by draining and start by curing the pus-filled sore until it becomes clean. Then resume the work as before, until it becomes clean again.
Et se li apparance de la chair dou larmier nuit en l’oil par grant nuisement, si la sospent a l’oncine, et en cope une partie et non mie tot, que cors de larmes n’i viegne;	And if the appearance of the flesh from the corner affects the eye with great harm, suspend it in vinegar, and carve out only part of it, not all at once, so that no tears come.
puis distille en l’oil coliere rouge qui est fais de litargire.	Then drop the red neckring which is made of silver into the eye.
de la char qui naist sus la prunelle	of the flesh that forms near the pupil
Es eulz d’aucuns homes naist aucune fois char rouge, et cuevre la prunele et restraint sus les papieres et les torne au defuer, et semble une rose de balauste;	There are some who have the eyes of certain people born with a red eye, covering the pupil and remaining on the paper and turning outside, seeming like a sapphire rose;
et li ovraiges si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz, et coil toute celle char as uncines convenaubles a ceu, et la sostien a la force;	And the procedures are such that the patient puts their head into your hand, then move their eyes, and do this to all parts of the body, ensuring each movement is coordinated with what you're doing, and hold them with strength.
puis cope la premiere char, et vai tout copant au raseur jusc’a la fin, et te garde que tu ne bleces l’oil a l’ovraige;	Then start with the first part of the body and move to shave it all off until the end of the process, making sure not to hurt the eye during this task.
et soit li incision dou spatumile que nos avons dit en l’incision de l’ungle et as petites forces de coi on oste lou sebel, si com li forme aprés cest chapistre lou demostre;	Make the cut like what we have described for the cut in the nail and with the small movements of your hands when dealing with bone, just as the figure shown after this chapter illustrates;
et quant li incision est acomplie et ostee toute li char, si emple l’oil de seil broiet ou tu i distille coliere rouge et semblans medicines corrosives, et met sus l’oil defuer coton avec abin d’uef, si qu’il soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut;	And when the cut is completed and all the flesh has been removed, use turpentine oil or distill it into red colander and similar corrosive medicines, then place cotton soaked with this oil outside where heat can be applied to promote healing.
et s’il i demore rien, et li sans chaus te sormonte, et tu doutes aposteme chaut, si laisse l’oil et cure l’aposteme de choses apaisant aposteme chaut;	And if it stays still, and you can feel a lump under the skin, and you doubt about an abscess, leave the eye alone and treat the abscess with things that soothe an abscess;
puis revien a ton ovraige tant qu’il soit sanez, et ensi fai cant chars est ajostee en l’oil par ceste semblance.	Then return to your work as long as it is clean, and thus make several characters attached inside the eye by this resemblance.
Mais toutevoie il covient que tu aliges la cure de chescun oil foible de la voie natureil;	However, nevertheless, it must be that you adjust the treatment of each natural weak eye;
et de la voie accident, en ovraige de fer;	and of the injured way, in the work of iron;
et ne bouter mie ta main en aucun de ces ovraiges tant que tu voies que cist membres soit soffrans celui ovraige.	and do not leave your hand in any of these works until you see that this limb endures that work.
des voines des eulz	of veins and eyes
Sebel sont voinnes rouges que sont covertes sus l’oil, et tolent a la veue son ovraige et afoiblissent l’oil toz jors.	When there are red veins covered over the eyes, they tolerate their work and weaken the sight for several days.
Mestier est donques au premier que tu regardes se li oil, en coi sebel est, est fors, et n’i a autre maladie fuers que lou sebel;	Thus the profession is at first to look where there might be a lump, in which it belongs, and besides, and there is no other disease besides that lump;
adonques le coil en teil maniere:	Therefore, perform this treatment like so:
comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain, puis sospent celles voines a tout l’oncine selonc sa sapience, et soit li oncines subtilz double selonc ceste forme:	Instruct the patient to put their head in good health, then suspend all their veins throughout the body according to their wisdom, and have the sinews be finely doubled according to this shape:
Et soient dui oncine par degrez en .i. cors selonc ceste forme:	And let there be two ounces in stages through one half according to this form:
puis c’on coil as forces celles voinnes subtilment, et essue lou sanc houre aprés autre, tant que tu voies removoir celles voines fuers de l’oil;	then carefully guide those fine veins, and let blood flow out the hour after another, until you see those veins being removed from the eye;
et garde que tu ne blecier l’oil as pointes des spatumiles, et fai cest ovraige a houre de midi devant lou soleil, et soies mout fervans en ton ovraige si que tu ne copes fuer que celles voinnes;	and make sure not to damage the eye at the tips of splinters, and do this operation in midday sun, and be very diligent in your work so that you only remove the veins.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si distille en l’oil coliere vert et rouge por corrumpre ceu qui est demorez dou sebel.	And when you have done this, if you drip a necklace of green and red in the eye to corrupt what remains due to congestion.
Et se tu n’as pooir de coillir tout ceu en celle houre, si fai emplastre sus l’oil de choses apaisans la dolor des eulz, et le laisse aucuns jors tant que li dolors soit apaisie et soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut, puis rencomence selonc ceste maniere qui est devant tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if you don't have the ability to treat it at that hour, make a plaster for the eye with things that soothe the pain of the eyes, and let it be for several days until the pain is soothed and assurance can be taken that there's no pus accumulation, then start again following this method until they are healed.
et c’est li forme des forces:	And this is the form of strength:
de la fistule de l’oil	Of the ear canal
Li mire si nomment «arissati» fistule:	The stent so called "arissati" is a fistula:
quant tu la cures per cautere et par medicine ague ardant selonc ceu que j’ai devant dit, et elle n’est mie sanee, si est engien en li que tu fendes sus l’aposteme, lai ou il doit meurer, et trai toute la moistor que i est, tant que li os soit descovers.	When you treat it with cautery and hot medicine according to what I have said before, and if it does not heal, then it is infected in the place you cut into the abscess, where it should die, and drain all the moisture that there is, until the bone is exposed.
Et quant li os iert descovers, et tu verras la corruption et la noiror, si la reis a tout l’estrument de coi ci est li forme;	And when the bone is fully exposed, and you see the decay and darkness, if you remove it with all the tool that I described;
et est apelez «aspre chief», et soit fait de feir inde a I chief reont, et soit pointoiez si com une lime si com il est en la presente forme:	And call it "hard head", and shape it from iron inside the head ring, and make its points like a file as it is in this form:
Et met sus lou leu de l’os corrumput, puis le torne entre tes dois, et presse ta main un poc tant que tu saiches que celle corruption est rese;	And place your fingers on the affected bone, then turn it between your thumbs, and press your hand a bit as long as you know that this corruption is removed;
et fai ceu aucune fois, puis restoure lou leu de medicines exiccatives.	And do this once, then restore the affected area with medicine that has been prepared for drying.
se li leus est soudez, et char i naist, et li cors de la bowe est soudez, et remaint ensi XL jors, et il ne renovele et n’est mie apostemez, et accidens mavais n’i vient, saiches qu’il est sanez;	When the muscles are joined, and there is a new birth of flesh, and the veins of the arm are joined, and remains like this for 40 days, and it does not heal nor becomes abscessed, and no bad accidents come about, know that it is cured;
se ceu non, si n’i a autre engien que de ramener la fistule au pertus dou neif selonc ceste forme:	If this does not work, so long as there is no other matter than to bring the fistula back to the neck of the nose according to this form:
et est que tu descuevre de l’os la seconde fois par fer, et par medicines agues, et quant il iert descovers si prent I foret selonc ceste forme, et soit li chiés de fer a III angles, et li fust soit atenuis jusc’a chief si com tu vois ci:	And when you uncover the bone for the second time with iron and through wet medicines, and when it is uncovered, take the cut according to this form, and place the iron point of three angles, and the shaft should be thinned up until its head as shown here:
puis le met sus l’os delez lou larmier, et esloigne ta main de l’oil I poc, puis torne a tot le foret tant qu’il perce l’os et le sent li malaides par ceu que li vens en ist s’il tient sa main sus son neif;	Then place the metal against the bone in the eyebrow area, and keep your hand away from the eye socket for a moment, then turn back to fully apply pressure until it pierces the bone. The patient will feel pain because of the wind entering through that point as long as you hold your hand on their nose;
et pues restoure lou leu de medicines seches, si com je t’ai ensigniet, et quant li char naist et endurcist li leus, si vait li matiere au neif;	And then restore the limb with dry medicines, as I have taught you, and when the sweat begins to appear and harden the skin, let the matter drain out of the nose;
si est plus legiere chose au malaide.	if it's something lighter for the patient.
de l’issue de l’oil	From the outcome of the eye
Quant li eulz apert fuer dou tout en tout, et il ne vient point de destorbier au nef, ne amenuisement, si covient que tu lies lou malaide;	When the eyes open fully and completely, and there is no dislocation or thinning of the lung, you should bind the patient;

et li maniere des drapelz si est que tu preignes drapelz assez molz, et double chescun en IIII, et puis met l’un sus l’autre selonc la quantiteit que li eulz en ait mestier;	And the method of folding the cloths is that you take cloths sufficiently soft, and double each one in four, and then place them one on top of another according to the amount they require.

puis oste lou liien aprés le jor et la nut, et se tu vois l’oil repairier, c’est boin;	Then check the bandage after day and night, and if you see the eye healing, that is good;
se ce non;	if not;
si rencomence l’emplaustre et les drapelz et lou liien et les ventouses tant qu’il soit sanez.	then redo the plaster, cloths, and bandage along with the suction cups until it heals.
dou derrompement de toile uvee	from the bursting of a blood clot
Quant disruptions vient en la toile uvee, puis apert, et vient fuer des papieres si com I grain de resins, et est espoantauble a veoir;	When tears come to the iris cloth, then open, and come out like pieces of resin, and is unbelievable to see;

puis l’estrai tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then remove it as soon as it has healed.
de la bowe de l’oil	From the field of the eye
Ceste maladie qui est apelee «alcunnati» nen est fuers que bowe qui est assemblee en l’oil, semblant a aigue dessendant, et ce n’est mie aigue;	This disease, which is called "alcunnati", can only be found where blood that resembles descending water accumulates in the eye, and it is not real water;
et li maniere de l’apparance de l’ovraige si est que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege appareilliet et droit, puis prent le chief entre tes mains de II pars, et lou muef tant que tu voies la bowe venir au desus a tes eulz;	And the way this disease appears is that you make the patient sit upright on an apparatus and straight, then take their head between your hands from both sides, and move them until you see the blood come up to your eyes.
puis soit ens fichie, et ne dessende et soit descombree li lumiere, et voie li malaides les choses si com il soloit;	Then let it burn, do not descend and let light disappear, behold the wounds as they should be.
et s’elle ne dessent desoz, saiches que c’est aigue, et se li dessendemens de la bowe n’est appareilliez si com nos avons dit.	And if it does not descend at once, know that it is severe, and if its descent from the eye isn't as we have said.

et quant elle ert issue, si distille en l’oil aigue chaude mellee a miel, ou aigue ou fenugreic est boillis et miel, puis soit curee d’autre cure tant qu’elle soit sanee. des aigues de l’oil	From tears of the eye
Nos avons jai les semblances des aigues en la division, et ceu qu’il covient por percier;	We have the indications for the use of water in division and what needs to be pierced;
si en oevre selonc la santeit.	if conducted according to health.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains croisiet, fuers de la lumiere por le soleil, et li lie l’oil sain et estreint mout fort;	It is necessary that you place the patient between your crossed hands, away from light in front of the sun, and tie the healthy eye tightly but not too tight.
puis met la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre se li eulz est senestres, ou a ta main destre se li eulz est destres;	then place the paper of the eye on your left hand if the eyes are opposite each other, or on your right hand if the eyes are side by side;
puis prent en ta main destre, se li eulz est senestres, l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda», ou a ta main senestre, se li eulz est destre;	then take in your right hand, if the eyes are opposite each other, the instrument called "almagda", or in your left hand if the eyes are side by side;

et covient que li mesure de la voie almagda soit au parfont de la mesure des l’espaice qui est des la prunele jusc’a la fin de la noirour;	And it is necessary that the measurement of the conduit amygadal be at the fullness of the measurement of the space which exists from the corner to the end of the darkness;
et c’est li corone de l’oil;	And it is the crown of the eye;
si verras l’os en celle papiere por la clarteit de la toile cornee, et pues met l’estrument jusc’a leu ou li aigue est, puis l’espresse desoz une voie aprés autre.	You will see the bone in that paper due to the transparency of the corneal fabric, and then place the tool up to it where its sharpness is, then express through one channel after another.
se li aigue dessent maintenant, si voit li malaides devant lui et l’estrument en son oil.	Let the patient now feel it descending, so they see the wounds before them and the instrument in their eye.
Aprés repose I petit, et se li aigue remonte la seconde voie, met la fuer avec l’estrument, et quant elle est ens fichie et ele ne monte, si estrai almagda legierement en tornoiant ta main poc et poc;	After having the patient lie down, and if the sharpness ascends on the second channel, apply force with the tool, and when it is firmly in place and no longer rises, then gently remove the amygadal tissue by twisting your hand slowly.

Nos, et cil qui sont de nostre tens, mettons sus comin broiet avec abun d’uef.	Yes, and those which belong to our type, place them on a common grid with plenty of egg white.
Et se almagda n’i puet entrer en l’oil par sa duresce, car il i a de teilz homes qui ont trop durs les eulz, si covient que tu preignes l’estrument qui est apelez «alberit», de coi ci est li forme:	And if almagda cannot enter the eye due to its hardness, for there are some people whose eyes are too hard, then it is necessary that you take the tool called 'alberit', of which here is its form:

puis le deslie en cele maison meisme tenebrouse, et esprueve sa veue, et lou fai veoir aucunes choses, et puis li remet lou lien jusc’a septime jor;	Then let them move within that dark house, and test their sight, and make sure they see nothing, and then place the bandage again until the seventh day;
et ne covient mie que tu faices ceu en l’oure de la cure ou aprés l’incision maintenant, mais il covient que tu aliges ceu, por ceu que li aigue monte hastanment.	And it is not right that you perform this during the time of the treatment or after incision now, but you should apply this because the fever rises quickly.
se apostemes chaus vient, que tu desliies l’oil devant le septime jor, et l’adrece de ceu qui assouaige aposteme;	For the removal of abscesses, you should cut it open on the seventh day, and then remove the pus from him who heals the abscess;
et quant il est apaisiez, si deslie la veue et met sus sa faice I orilliet por covrir aucun jor, et soit adés en celle maison tenebrouse.	And when it is relieved, you should release the eye and place it above its socket with a little gold to cover for one day, and then stay in that dark house.

et saiches que nulz deciples ne se doit entremettre en cest cas.	Know that no disciples should interfere in this situation.
Et uns vint a nos qui estoit de la Yrach, qui nos dist que en som pais faisoit om almagda perciet, a coi on succe l’aigue, mais toutevoie je n’en vis onques nul en nostre terre, ne je ne lou lis onques en livres des anciens;	And one came to us who was from the East, who told us that elsewhere they would make gold into silver, by which one can transform water, but nevertheless I never saw anyone do this in our land, nor have I ever read about it in ancient books;
et par aventure c’est une novele chose.	And perhaps this is something new.

de la char sor le neis	Of the flesh around the nose

et si i a de telz ou il ait char enchancree de fuxe color, et si a char souef de bone color.	And if there are such or if it has a mixed char with red color, and if it has a well-colored char.

et c’est li forme de l’estrument por purgier lou chief, a coi on distille les oiles et les medicines ou neis:	And this is the form of the instrument for purging the head, to which one distills oils and medicines or on the nose:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, semblant a une lampe overte, si com une cainne, et li conduis ausi;	And it should be made of silver or iron, resembling an open lamp or a cane, and guide it in the same manner;

et ait I mainche au chief por lou tenir quant on chaufe l’oile ou aucune liquor.	and have your hand ready on the head so that when you heat the oil or any liquid, it doesn't move.
de la char sor le neis	Of the flesh around the nose
Maintes fois naist au chief dou neis une maladie qui est apelee «telul», et croist et devient grans adés, tant qu’il est vis chose au regarder;	Many times, in the head under the nose, a disease is born which is called "Telul," it grows and becomes large enough to be seen;
et por ceu covient que tu lou copes au comencement, et l’oste tout fuer, puis met sor leu lou cautere ou la medicine ardant;	And because of this, you should prepare the wound at the beginning, and heat up the bone completely, then place either the cautery or the burning medicine onto it;
et s’on le tarde a coper tant qu’il soit grans, si pren warde s’il est durs, de fuxe color, de povre sens:	And if you delay to cover it until it is large, take care if it is hard, if it changes color, or if it has poor sensation:
si ne lou touchier mie de fer car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, car quant on le cope aucune fois, si en vient grant malice au malaide;	If you do not touch it with iron at all because it is a trapped abscess, for when one cuts it once, it causes great discomfort to the patient;

quant li neis est copez et cosus	When the nose has been cut and sewn together

des apostemes des levres	from abscesses of lips

de la char des gencives	of the flesh of the gums
Maintes fois naist sus les gencives char ajostee, que li ancien apelent «albulus»;	Many times, something white arises on the gum that is adhered to the tooth, which the old would call "albulus";
si covient que tu la sostienes as tenailles, et la cope a sa racine, et laisse corre la bowe ou le sanc;	So you must hold it with the forceps and remove it at its root, and leave to cure where blood or blood has flowed.
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet, ou autres poudres restraignans et desiccatives;	Then place on the wound vitriol powder or other drying and desiccating powders;
et se celle char revient aprés l’incision, et maintes fois avient, si la cope la seconde fois, et la cauterize:	And if this flesh returns after the incision and happens repeatedly, if you cut it a second time, and apply cautery:
si ne revient mie aprés le cautere;	if it does not return after the cautery;
et ce sont les formes des estrumens por coper.	and these are the forms of instruments to be used.
des sordens	Of cauteries made with fire, command the sick person to let their hairs grow long and even; and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Aucunes fois sont assemblees au chief des dens, dedens la bouche entre les gencives, escorces qui sont laides et aspres;	Sometimes they gather at the root of the teeth, inside the mouth between the gums, with scaly and rough layers.
et aucune fois sont li dent noir et citrin et vers, tant que li corruption vient a la gencive, et sont li dent puant;	And sometimes they come together as black and yellow teeth with worms, until the decay reaches the gums, and the teeth stink.
si covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, et ses chiés soit en ton saint, et reis les dens ou les escorces aperent, tant qu’il n’i demore rien;	It is necessary that you place the patient between your hands, and their head in your holy direction, and pull out the teeth or scales until nothing remains.
et ensi fai de la noiror et de la verdor, et de la jaunice et des autres taiches, tant qu’elles soient mondees;	And thus make it black and green, and yellow and other shades, until they are all removed.
et s’on oste ceu que i est a la premiere rasion, c’est boin;	And if we remove what is at the first reason, it's good;
se ceu non, si rencomence a rere le secont jor et lou tier, tant que tu aies tout reis;	But if not, start again from the second day and the third, until you have everything taken care of;
et saiches que li dent ont mestier de diverses formes d’estrumens por reire, selonc ceu que li oevre lou demoustre, por ceu que li raseur dont on reit defuer les dens ont autres formes que cil dont on reit entre les dens;	And know that teeth require various types of instruments to work, according to what the procedure demonstrates, because the root that comes out of the gum has other shapes than those that come between the teeth;
et cestes formes et autres soient avec toi appareillies.	And these forms and others be prepared with you.
Il covient quant tu cures lou dent de sa dolor que tu tardes dou traire tant com tu pues, car ce ne doit om mie faire;	It is necessary that when you cure the tooth of its pain, you keep the tool as long as possible, because it should not hurt at all;
car c’est une substance mout haute jusc’a donc c’on n’ait point d’excusation dou raier.	because this is a very sensitive substance thus one should not have any excuse for the irritation.
Adonques quant li malaides est constrains dou traire, si covient que tu soies certains dou dent doillant.	So when the patient is constrained to bleed, it must be certain as to which vein to pierce.
Maintes fois desoit li dolor lou malaide, et cuide qu’elle soit ou dent saint, et fait traire le boin dent;	Many times during a person's illness, and fearing it might be toothache, and believing it to be holy toothache, they would draw the pus out of the good tooth;
et toutevoie ne se depart mie li dolor per ceu, tant que li malvais estrais, car nos l’avons ja veut faire a ces sainors;	And yet, they never leave the pain alone for such reasons, until the evil is removed, because we have already seen fit to do this among the soldiers;
et quant tu es bien certains dou dent doillant, si covient que tu escorches entor lou dent a tout i. spatumile fort por warder la gencive de toutes pars;	And when you are quite sure of the tooth causing pain, it is necessary that you cauterize around the tooth to all half inches thick in order to keep the gum from spreading everywhere;
puis le mues a tes dois ou as tenailles subtilz au premier poc et poc, tant qu’il soit bien eslochiés, puis i afferme bien les tenailles;	Then move it with your hands or by the use of fine tongs at each click and click, until they are well locked in place, then firmly secure the tongs;
et soit li chiés dou malaide en ton saint entre tes genous, et lou tien bien si qu’il ne se mueve.	And have the head of the illness in your holy place between your knees, and hold it well so that it does not move.
Aprés estrai lou dent droitement sens brisier, et s’il ne saut fuer, si prent aucun de ces estrumens et le boute dedens de chescune part legierement, et lou remuef si com tu as fait premier.	After extracting the right tooth correctly without breaking it, and if it does not jump out, take none of these tools and push them inside each part gently, and move it in the same way you did first.
Et se li dens est perciez et mengiez, si covient que tu l’emplisses de drapelz, lai ou li pertus sont;	And if it is pierced and eaten, you should fill them with cloths where they were lost;
et si l’estraint subtilment as tenailles, que il ne brise a l’estraindre;	and if it is gently squeezed with tongs, so that it does not break while being squeezed;
et covient mout saigement ovrer entor la gencive por deschaucier lou dent.	It must be opened quite carefully between the gum for the extraction of the tooth.
Et te done bien en warde que tu ne le brises, et en remaigne une partie, et reveigne au malaide par la malice de la racine plus grans dolors de la premiere.	And make sure you do not break it well, and leave a part of the tooth, awaken the patient to greater pain from the root than at first due to its cleverness.
Et te warde que tu ne faices mie ensi com font li ignorant sainor, qui par lor haste et par lor hardiesce brisent aucune fois le charreit, et n’i amenistrent mie ceu que nos avons conteit;	And beware that you do not act this way as the ignorant surgeons do, who break the bone every time due to their haste and boldness, and do not bring in what we have told you;
mais font venir aucune fois par l’oquison de ceu grant maladie por les racines que i demorent, ou por lou charreit qu’il brisent, si com nos avons sovent veut;	but bring it once by the extraction of this great disease due to the roots that remain, or due to the bone they break, as we have often done;
et quant li dens est trais, si lavez lou leu de vin ou d’aisil et de seil;	And when the teeth are pulled, if you wash the mouth with wine or salt or vinegar;
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, que sovent avient, si emple lou leu de vitriole broiet;	And when bleeding occurs during this process, which often happens, if you use vinegar instead for washing;
et se ceu ne vaut, si le cauterize.	And if that doesn't work, then apply the cautery.
Les formes des estrumens, a coi om muet les dens premier, soient a longes pointes et a gros mainches, qu’il ne doublent mie quant tu trairas le dent;	The shape of the tools you use to remove teeth should be such that they have long points and large handles; this way, they won't bend when you are pulling out the tooth.
et ce sont les formes:	And these are their shapes:
Et soient de gros membres si qu’il ne ploient mie au traire, et soient de fer inde bien fait, et soient dentez por mues tenir.	And may have large members that do not bend when being pulled, and be made of well-crafted iron, and have teeth for holding as needed.
de la racine des dens	from the root of the teeth
Quant li racine demoure au traire, si covient que tu mettes sor le leu coton moilliet em burre I jor ou II, tant que li leus soit amolis, pues i boute les tenailles qui sont apelees «algefri», de coi li chiés semblet bec de soigne;	When the root remains after extraction, it is necessary to place cotton soaked in butter or oil inside the mouth for one or two days until the wound heals. This allows you to use forceps called "algefi" which makes the patient seem like they are being taken care of;
et soient dedens faites ausi com une lime et c’est li forme:	And they should be made as within a file, for this is its form:
Et se les racines ne vuellent issir a tout ces tenailles, si covient que tu descuevre la char tot entor la racine, et i met l’estrument qui est apelez «althali», c’est a savoir palainche, de coi ci est li forme:	And if they do not want to come out of all these nails, it is necessary that you reveal the flesh entirely along the root and place the tool called "althalus", which means palanchet, as its form is shown here:
Et soit fors et gros si qu’il ne brise mie, et se li racine saut par ceu, c’est boin;	And let it be strong and thick so that it does not break, and if its root jumps out of this, it is good;
se ceu non, si t’aide de toz les estrumens, de coi les formes vienent ci aprés:	If not, assist with all instruments, from which the following forms come:
Et si s’aide on de cest estrument qui ait .ij. rains, de coi ci est li forme:	And if one uses this tool which has two points, as its form is shown here:
et d’autres ferremens qui sont devant en la rasion des dens, et de cest estrument qui semble unes grans tenailles, dont ci est li forme:	and there are other tools placed according to the order of teeth, and this tool that appears to be large tweezers, as its form is shown here:
Et soit cist estrumens fors qu’il ne puisse brisier, et saiches que mout d’estrumens de dens sont;	And let these instruments be strong so that they cannot break, and know that very few bone-breaking instruments exist;
et ausi d’autres estrumens, qui ne sont mie contez;	And also other instruments, which are not even mentioned;
et li saiges maistres subtilz trueve par soi meisme son estrument, selonc ceu que ses ovraiges et li maladie li demoustre, car il i a de teilz maladies ou li ancien n’enseignerent point d’estrument por la diversiteit d’au;s et s’om brise point dou charreit ou des autres os, ou il porrit, si i cerche as estrumens qu’il i covient, que je t’ai dit, et t’aide des gestes, de coi ci est li forme:	And the wise masters find their own instrument by themselves, according to what their works and disease indicate to them. For there are parts of diseases where the old ones did not teach any instruments due to the diversity among others, or if it breaks part of the body or other bones, or if it rots, so they search for the appropriate tools that I have mentioned and help with gestures; this is their form:
Et soient gros et bien tenant por tenir l’os, qu’il n’eschaipe, mais le puisse tenir et oster;	And make them large and firmly holding for holding the bone, so it does not escape, but can hold and remove;
et puis restoure lou leu de medicines convenant a ceu, et s’il ait en l’os porriture, et elle est petite, si la reis a tout cest estrument:	and then restore the right side with suitable medicines for this, and if there is decay in the bone and it is small, if you insert all of this instrument to it:
Quant li dent apperent ne mie selonc lou cors natureil, et li forme est laide, et meismement en femmes puceles, si covient que tu saiches se li dens est neis aprés lou dent, et n’est mie en droit leu, et on ne lou puet soier ne limer:	When the tooth does not appear as natural to the body, and its shape is ugly, even in virgins, you must know whether the tooth was born after the tooth, and it is not in its right position, and one cannot see or file it:
adonques lou raie;	then the groove;
et s’il est aers avec lou dent, si prent cest estrument dont ci est li forme, et est semblans a I petit bec, et soit de fer inde agut en som:	and if it is next to the tooth, take this instrument as described above, and it resembles a small beak, and it should be made of steel that remains sharp:
Et lou cope poc et poc em mains jors por la duresce dou dent, et por ceu que tu ne mueves les autres, et s’il est apparans c’on le puisse limer, si lou lime d’une teil lime com ci est li forme:	And the tooth is inserted gradually into one's hand due to its hardness and because you don't move others, and if it can be seen that we could grind it, then this tooth is ground with a single grinding wheel as it is formed:
et est ausi com li lime de coi on fait les aguilles;	And also like the iron used to make needles;
et en lime lou dent poc et poc em mains jors legierement, si qu’il ne se mueve tant qu’il chiece;	And with the file on his teeth, tapping lightly in my hands, so that it does not move until it breaks;
puis la plaine en la fin a tout aucun raseur, et se li dens est trop trenchans et il blece la lengue, si covient limer l’aspreteit tant qu’il soit igalz, si qu’il ne blece la lengue ne ne corrompe la parole.	Then in the end on all smoothing tools, and if it's too sharp and it hurts the tongue, it's necessary to smooth down the roughness until it's even, so that it doesn't hurt the tongue nor corrupt speech.
quant li dent lochent	when the tooth becomes loose
Quant li dent devant lochent, ou par percussion ou par cheoir, et li malaides ne puet presser sus ceu qu’il menjue qu’il ne chient, et tu les as curez de medicines restrignans, et ceu ne vaut;	When the front teeth are struck or through impact, and if the patient doesn't vomit what he eats when they don't leak, and you've treated them with restricting medicines, then it's not valid;
si les covient restraindre d’un fil d’or, car li filz d’argent devient vert et porrit, mais li ors ne se mue onques;	if they need to be restrained by a gold thread, for silver threads turn green and rot, but gold never changes.
et soit li filz moiens ne trop gros ne trop menus, selonc la quantiteit de l’espaice entre les dens;	And let the children neither too large nor too small, according to the size of the gap between the teeth;
et se tu vues adrecier les dens, si pren lou fil et lou boute double entre les II dens sains, puis met les chiés entre les dens meus, s’il en i a I ou plusors, tant que tu veignes saigement jusc’au dent sain d’autre part;	And if you see the teeth moving, take the thread and the needle doubled between the two healthy teeth, then place the head between the molar teeth, as long as there is another tooth that feels properly to the healthy tooth on the other side;
puis rencomence la coverture jusc’a la partie ou tu encomensas, et estrains ta main subtilment et saigement, tant qu’il ne se mueve point;	Then continue the dressing until you reach the part where you stopped, and gently and carefully tighten your hand, as long as it does not move at all;
et soit ta lieeure a la racine dou dent si qu’il ne puist eschaper.	And tie your thread to the root of the tooth so that it cannot escape.
Puis cope les chiés dou fil a unes tenailles, et les assemble, et les repont entre le dent sain, et le met ensi qu’il ne blece la lengue;	Then grip the heads with tweezers, and align them, placing them back between the healthy tooth, making sure they do not irritate the tongue;
et puis le laisse ensi estroit tant com il puet demorer, et s’il deslie, ou li filz ront, si l’estraint d’un autre fil;	And then let it stay slightly restricted like it can endure for some time, and if it slips or the bands come undone, if they need to be held tight by another band;
si demorrait et servira ensi tout son tens, et c’est li forme des dens et li figure de l’adrecement des II dens sains, et des II meus, si com tu vois:	if it could endure for the entire time, and this is the shape of the roots and the arrangement of the healthy second roots and the diseased second roots as you see:
Et quant li dent chiet, si lou remet on en son leu, de fres en fres, si com nos avons dit;	And when the tooth falls out, if it's removed and placed back in its original position step by step, as we have said;
et ne s’en entremette mie qui n’est saiges et soffrans, et aucune fois fait on la forme d’un dent d’os de vaiche, et lou met on au leu ou li defaute est, et l’estraint on si com nos avons dit, et demore et sert ensi lonc tens.	And don't try to replace it with anything inappropriate that can cause harm and never make the shape of an ox's bone tooth; instead, place it back at its rightful spot where there is a defect, hold it in place as we have described, and let it remain and serve for as long as necessary.
de coper lou liien de la lengue	covering the wound of the tongue
Aucune fois est cist liiens qui vient desoz la lengue ou naturez, que on naist ensi;	No time does it come from within the tongue or nature, so one is born thus;
ou par accident de plaie soudee;	or by chance of a缝ed wound;
et li ovraiges est telz que tu oevre la bouche dou malaide, et ait sa teste en ton sain, et li lieve la lengue;	and the actions are such that you work at the mouth with the aid, have your head in good health, and lift the tongue;
puis cope lou liien nervous dou large, tant que li lengue soit desloie de son tenement, et se il i a duresce ou nout, et c’est de soudement de plaie, si i boute l’uncine et cope dou large celui liement;	then cut the nervous bundle from the base, until the tongue is dislocated from its place, and if there is hardness or lack, this is a sudden wound, so force the hook and cut from the base that connection;
et garde que li fendure ne soit mie trop em parfont, por l’artere qui est desoz;	and make sure the incision is not too deep by mistake, for there is an artery underneath;
et quant tu as fait, si leve le leu d’aigue rose et d’aisil, ou d’aigue froide, puis met desoz la lengue une tente de lin;	and when you have done so, if lift the wound that is pink and moist or cool, then put under the tongue a linen tent;
et la teigne li malaides chescune nuit, que li leus ne puisse soder.	And the disease afflicts the patient every night, so that his limbs cannot bear it.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si met sor le leu vitriole broiet;	And when bloodletting occurs, place the blistering iron over the affected area;
et se li sans te vaint, si le cauterize au cautere lentiginout, qui est boin a ceu;	And if it doesn't heal with that, apply the slow-acting cautery to it, which is good for such cases;
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez,	Then continue other treatments until they are healed,
et se tu lou vois de fusse color ou noir ou dur, si que li malaides ne lou sent, si n’i touchier point, car c’est chancre;	And if you see that it has turned red or black or hard, so that the patient doesn't feel it, do not touch it at all, because this is gangrene;
et s’il est declinans a blenchor, et il i a moistor, si i giete l’oncine, et lou fent d’un spatumile subtil, et lou delivre d’une part et d’autre;	And if it is deteriorating to the point of pus formation, and there is moisture present, then use vinegar, and apply a subtle poultice, and cure from both sides;
et se li sans te vaint a ton ovraige, si met sus vitriole broiet tant qu’il soit estainchiez, puis revien a ton ovraige tant que tu traies tout fuer;	And if you can't find it in your work, then apply vinegar to it until it's clean, then return to your work as long as you're extracting all force;
puis leve lou leu d’aisil et de seil, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then lift up the aid and sail, and perform other treatments until it becomes clean.
des apostemes de la gorge	regarding throat abscesses
Aucune fois vient dedens la gorge boces qui sont apelees «godath», et les apele on proprement les II amandres, et quant tu les cures, si com nos avons dit en la division, et elles ne sont sanees, si pren garde:	None of the nodes inside the throat called "godaths" come into being. They are correctly named as the two almonds, and when you treat them, just like what we have said in the division, and they are not healed, then take care:
se c’est apostemes dur de petit sens et de fusse color, si ne lou touchier mie de fer.	If it's hard pus of little sense and colored, don't touch it with iron.
Et s’il est rouges et li racine est grosse, si ne lou touchier mie de fer, ausi por lou decorrement de sanc;	And if it's red and the root is large, don't touch it with iron either, for the circulation of blood;
mais lou laisse tant qu’il soit meur, et adonques tu lou partiras, ou il rompirait par soi;	But let it until it is heated, then you will take it away, or it would break by itself;
et s’il est de blainche color reont, et li racine est subtilz, si aies apareilliet l’estrument por coper, mais regarde premierement se li apostemes chalz repose et est apaisiez.	And if it has a whiteish hue and the root is delicate, when you have prepared your instrument for use, but first check that the abscess cavity has cooled down and is calm.
Adonques fai seoir lou malaide devant lou soleil, et ses chiés soit en ton sain, et li oevre la bouche et lou preigne li serjans entre ses mains, et presse la lengue desoz a tout l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme;	Then have the patient face the sun and keep their limbs warm. Let them open their mouth and place the surgeon's hands on their tongue, pressing it all along the instrument, as this is how it should be done;
et soit d’argent ou d’arain subtil ausi com uns coutelz:	And may it be made of fine silver or steel, as sharp as knives:
Cant tu presses la lengue a tout cest estrument, et tu vois l’aposteme, si pren l’oncine et lou fiche en l’amandre, et la trai fuer au desus plus que tu pues;	Can you press the tongue against this entire instrument? And you see the abscess. If so, take the thimble and insert it into the almond-shaped area, pressing harder than you can with your fingers;
et trai aucune chose des toiles avec, puis la cope a l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme, que semble unes forces;	And take nothing from the cloth with you, then apply the paste to the tool, of which this is the shape, that seems like some strength;
et toutevoie li chief sont corbé, et l’un endroit l’autre, et sont molt agut, et est fait de fer inde ou d’andainne:	And always the head is mended, one place after another, and it's very sharp, made of iron or steel:
Et se tu n’as cest estrument present, si lou cope as tenailles, de coi ci est li forme:	And if you do not have this tool present, then use forceps, as depicted here:
Et soit trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part nom;	And so be sharp on one side, and on the other also;
et quant tu as copeit l’une des amandres, si cope l’autre selonc cele meisme maniere, et aprés l’incision gargarize li malaides aigue chaude, et aigue et aisil, et se decorremens de sanc avient, si gargarize li malaides aigue, ou escorces de pomes grenates soient cuites, ou fuelles de mirte, et semblans choses, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And when you have applied the paste to one of the almonds, apply it to the other in the same manner. After incision, gargle the patient with hot and very warm water, and also with cold but still warm water, and if bleeding occurs, gargle them with cold water or slices of cooked pomegranate fruits, or bay leaves, or similar things, until the bleeding stops;
puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then proceed with the treatment as long as it is effective;
et aucune fois naissent en la gorge autres apostemes que les II amandres, si les cope donques ensi com les II amandres igament.	And no other abscesses are born in the throat except for those resembling almonds, if they are treated accordingly just like the two almonds.
Et je medicinai une femme d’un aposteme que li estoit neis dedens la gorge, c’est a savoir I aposteme de petit sens;	And I treated a woman with an abscess that was born inside her throat, which is commonly known as the small senseless abscess.
et avoit jai bien pres close toute la gorge, si que li femme ne pooit expirer por le conduit qui estoit estoupez, et ne pooit ne mengier ne boivre, et fust morte s’elle demorast ensi I jor ou II.	And it was so tightly closed off that all the woman's throat, she could not breathe through the blocked passage, and therefore could neither eat nor drink, dying if she had remained in this state for a day or two.
Et li apostemes estoit jai si montez qu’il avoit fuer mis II rains par les II pertuis dou neis.	And the abscesses had ascended so much that they had caused two rows of blisters under each nostril.
Je hastai donques tantost, et fichai en l’un I oncine, puis lou traï fuers, et en traï grant porcion de bowe;	I acted quickly then, piercing it with an awl, and then pulled out the thread, extracting a large portion of the pus;
puis refis autreteil en l’autre pertus dou neis, et li ovrai la bouche et li pressai la lengue;	Then I cut another piece under the other nostril, and on that one, I opened his mouth and pressed his tongue.
aprés fichai l’oncine en ces apostemes, et en copai une partie, et n’en issit fuers que un poc de sanc;	After removing the bile from these abscesses, and I took a part of it, yet only a little blood came out.
et ensi fut destoupez li conduis de la gorge la femme, et comensa maintenant a boivre aigue et puis vin, et ne cessai de taillier de cel aposteme par lonc tens;	And so the woman's throat duct was opened, and she began to drink water and then wine from this moment onwards; I didn't stop cutting that abscess for a long time.
et li apostemes recroissoit adés, et remplissoit lou leu que je avoie vuidiet, tant qu’il refut mout gros;	And the abscesses would recur immediately, filling up once more the area that I had emptied out, until it grew very large.
adonques je l’engignai et lou cauterizai dedens la gorge:	So I treated and cauterized inside the throat:
ensi demora sens croistre;	And it didn't grow again;
et me partis de ces parties, et ne soi que Deus fist de li aprés moi.	And I depart from these parts, and may God make of him after me.
de l’uve	regarding the eye
Quant reume dessent a l’uve, et elle est enflee et elle est longe, si est apelee «perpendiculaire»;	When it descends to the eye, and it becomes elongated, if it is called "perpendicular";
et s’elle est desoz grosse et reonde, si est apelee «uve».	And if it is large and round, it is called "eye".
Quant elle est curee si com nos avons dit en la division, et li cure ne profite mie, et tu vois que li chaus apostemes est apaisiez, et elle est subtilz, si covient que tu la copes;	When it is treated as we have said in the division, and the treatment does not benefit, and you see that the wound has calmed down and healed, and it becomes subtle, then it is necessary to apply it;
et celle qui est reonde assemblee et n’est mie longe;	And the one that is round and assembled, and is not lengthy;
et elle est sanguine ou de fusse color ou noire, si covient que tu eschues l’incision de li.	And if it is bloody or dark red or black in color, then it is necessary to avoid the incision of it.
Car il i a grant peril sus lou malaide.	For there is great danger for the patient.
Il covient donques, quant tu la vois, selonc la maniere que j’ai dit, de sa blenchor et de sa longesce, que tu faices seoir le malaide devant lou soleil, et li presse la lengue a l’estrument dont nos avons fait la remembrance ci devant;	So when you see the person it is necessary to do as I have said about their shape and length; make them stand in front of the sun, and press their tongue with the tool we mentioned earlier.
puis fiche l’oncine en l’uve, et la trai desoz, et la cope a I des II estrumens que j’ai dit en l’incision des II amandres.	Then press the anus into the abdomen, and proceed from there, and cut towards the second organ as I described in the incision of the two glands.
Et covient que tu ne coper mie fuer que la superfluiteit qui est outre le termine natureil;	So it is necessary that you do not cut more than the excess which extends beyond the natural boundary;
car se tu en copes plus, si grieves a la voix, et a la parolle;	for if you cut more, you will harm the voice and speech;
et aprés l’incision, use de ceu que nos avons dit en l’incision des II amandres, et le cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	After making the incision, use what we have explained about the incisions of the two glands, and treat until it has healed.
Et se li malaides a paor dou coper, si covient que tu i use d’engien a la cauterization de li sens paor.	And if the patients have fear about cutting, it is necessary that you apply means to their sense of fear in the process of cautery.
Et li maniere dou cautere si est aigue ague.	The way of cautery involves using an active instrument.
Et est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, et puis li presse la lengue a l’estrument que nos avons dit ou chapistre de cautere, et confis avec aigue vive chaus, si qu’elle ne soit mie trop espesse ne trop clere;	And let the patients place their head in your healthy position, and then press their tongue with the tool that we have mentioned or described in the chapter on cautery, and hold it firmly with sharp forceps, so that they are neither too thick nor too thin.
et en emple le chevement de cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme:	and when using the strength of this tool, as it is shaped:
Et ait ou chief une cheveure ou om met la medecine, si com li chevemens d’une cuillier, et met l’estrument a tout la medicine sus l’uve;	Have your head covered with a cloth or place the medicine there, like spreading on a spoon, and apply the tool evenly over the entire area.
et li malaides soit gisans sus son costeit, si que li salive et li muscillaige corre de sa bouche de la medicine dedens, si qu’ele ne dessende a la gorge, et lou blece;	And let the patient lie on their side so that saliva and mucus can drain from their mouth due to the medicine inside, ensuring it doesn't descend into the throat, causing choking.
puis tien ta main a tout la medicine et la presse sus l’uve, la quantiteit de la moitiet d’une houre, tant que tu la vois nercie et li mordications de la medicine soit apaisie;	Then hold your hand over the entire area of medicine and apply pressure to the affected area for half an hour, until you see it being absorbed and the irritation from the medicine is alleviated.
et se tu vues, pren coton et l’envoloupe sus aucun estrument, et moille lou coton en la medicine, et boute l’estrument a tout le couton en la cainne desus, tant que li coton s’aerde sus l’uve;	And if you see this, take cotton and cover it on any tool, and moisten the cotton in the medicine, then wrap the tool with all the cotton on top of the reed, until the cotton dries inside the organ.
et fai ceu sovent, tant que li cauteres soit parfais, puis la laisse elle seche, et chiet aprés IIII jors ou V.	And do this often, until the cauterization is perfect, then let it dry, and wash after three or five days.
Et se tu as mestier de rencomencier lou cautere de la medicine, si le rencomence, et aprés le cautere l’essue entor l’uve, de couton embut em burre, et mundifie ceu qui est entor de la medicine;	And if you need to repeat the medicinal cauterization, then do so, and after the cauterization go around inside the organ with it, using cotton dipped in butter, and clean the area that is inside of the medicine;
et soit arosez d’aigue froide, et soit curez de gargarismes tant qu’il soit sanez.	And let it be rinsed with cold water, and also do gargling until it is healed.
Ceste cure est plus save de l’incision, ne que li cautere;	This treatment is safer than cutting, nor does the cautery cause harm;
s’elle est curee de fumigation selonc ceste maniere, pren calament et ysope et origanum et rue et camomille et avronne et semblans herbes, et les assemble toutes ou aucunes d’eles en I pot, et i met aisil, et fai bullir;	If it is treated with fumigation in this manner, take chamomile, hyssop, and rue, as well as basil, camomile, parsley, and similar herbs. Gather all or some of these into a single pot, fill it up, and bring the contents to a boil;
et li potz soit bien gluez de fort terre, et enmi le pot ait I estrument cheveit selonc ceste maniere:	And ensure that the pot is well sealed with strong earth, and inside the pot place the heating tool according to this manner:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, et soit li uns des chiés boutez en la bouche dou malaide tant que li vapor monte a l’uve par la caine, tant que li uve soit mortifie;	And it should be made of silver or iron, and if one of the shoulder blades is placed in the mouth of the sick person until the vapor rises through the nose to the womb, as long as the womb is necrotic;
aprés lou rencomence sovent, tant que li uve seche, et garde que tu ne faices ceu au comencement de l’avenement de l’aposteme chaut, car plusors choses i avienent;	Afterward it often recurs, until the womb dries, and make sure you do not perform this at the beginning of the coming out of pus, for many things occur;
et ne faire mie ceu fuer que a la declination d’aposteme chaut.	And do not perform such action when there is an evacuation of pus from the abscess.
Et se cist estrument n’est presens, si pren une caine et met dedens lou chief une craiffe d’uef, si que li bouche au malaide n’ait mie trop chaut;	And if this instrument is not available, take a reed and put a piece of an eggshell inside the patient's mouth, so that the fire does not get too hot on the patient.
car li craiffe d’uef ne lait mie la vapor grever la bouche, et c’est bone cure ensamble salut.	For the eggshell does not produce heavy vapor in the mouth, and this is a good treatment combined for health.
Maintes fois s’aert a la gorge os ou espinee de poisson, ou aucune chose;	Many times it occurs in the throat bone or spine of fish, or nothing;
si covient donc que tu traies ceu que tu pues veoir, et li presse la lengue au soleil a tout l’estrument, si que tu voies mues la chose;	So it is necessary that you treat what you can see, and press the tongue to the sun with all the instrument, so that you see the thing move;
et ceu que ne t’apert mie et est reponus en la gorge, covient que tu faices vomir le malaide ainsois que li viande soit cuite en l’estomac;	And that which does not allow you to see it and is stuck in the throat, you should make the patient vomit this way that the meat be cooked in the stomach;
par aventure si istra li chose aerse par le vomissement;	By chance if it is pushed out by vomiting;
ou li malaides englutisse une piece d’esponge, ou une piece de navel, ou une racine de laitue, ou I morceil de pain sec;	or the patient swallows an sponge piece, or a belly button piece, or a lettuce root, or a fragment of dry bread;
et lie a l’esponge I fil, et puis la transglutisse;	and attaches to the sponge with a thread, and then swallows it.
et quant elle venra au leu, si s’aerdra, et puis trairas fuer;	and when it reaches its place, if it opens, and then expels force;
et s’elle ne vient fuer de ceu que nos avons dit, si pren I estrument de plonc selonc ceste forme:	and if it does not come out with the force that we have said, take an instrument of a plumber according to this shape:
Et soit li estrumens corbés au chief si qu’il puist plus legierement entrer en la gorge, et ait le chief en haut leveit;	And let the instruments be curved at the head so that it can enter more easily into the throat, and have the head raised in height;
et warde que tu ne touchier l’epiglote, que li tous ne li viegne, ne ne bouter mie l’os dedens;	and beware not to touch the epiglottis, lest all be obstructed, nor push any bone inside;
et mues vaut que li malaides i boute l’estrument, por ceu qu’il seit mues ou li chose est aerse;	And it is better for the patient to control the tool, because they should control or the thing becomes loose;
si la boute aval, ou il la traie fuer a tout l’estrument igalment, tant qu’elle soit fuer.	If the patient is breathing properly, or if they apply force evenly to all parts of the tool throughout, as long as they maintain their strength.
de la sansue de la gorge	from the saliva of the throat
Aucune fois est medicinee li sansue, si com j’ai dit en la division, par la cure de medicines;	There is no healing without surgery, as I have explained in the division, through the treatment of medicines;
et quant ceu ne profite mie, adonques regarde en la gorge dou malaide au soleil, puis que tu li presses la lengue a l’estrument que je t’ai dit.	And if this doesn't prove beneficial, then look into the throat of the patient towards the sun, and then have them press their tongue with the tool I've told you about.
Et se tu vois la sansue, si la trai a tout I petit uncine, ou as tenailles subtilz que valent a ceu.	And if you see blood, guide it out with every small fraction, or with fine tweezers that suffice for this purpose.
Et se ceu ne vaut, si pren une caine chevee, et la boute en la gorge dou malaide, puis boute ou chevement de la caine I fer chaut, et fai ce sovent.	And if this doesn't work, take a piece of a hair and push it into the throat of the patient, then remove or stop the bleeding with the end of the hair by twisting it. And do this often.
Et se teigne li malaides d’aigue toute jor.	And if you dye the patient's body with water throughout the day.
puis pren plein I voirre d’aigue froide, et oevre la bouche, et la giete ens sens englutir, et la mueve a sa main sovent;	Then take a full view of cold water and open their mouth, then pour it in gently without them swallowing it, and move it often with their hand.
et si tost com li sansue sent l’aigue, si chiet.	And as soon as one feels the cold like water, they die.
Et s’elle ne chiet si com nos avons dit, si subfumige lou malaide d’asefetide, a l’estrument que j’ai dit en la fumigation de l’uve;	And if it doesn't relieve as we have said, subdue the patient with asafetida, using the tool I mentioned in the section on asafetida application.
fai ceu maintes fois, car elle cherra sens targier.	Do this many times, for it will relieve without causing harm.
Et li maniere de la fumigation si est que tu preignes I pot ou il ait charbons vis, et soit li pos covert d’un coverseil perciet en mileu, et en celui pertus soit li chiés de l’estrument;	And the method of applying the heat involves taking an iron pot containing glowing charcoal, covering it with a thin lid in the middle, and placing the patient's head on that part.
puis i giete ta fumigation, et li malaides mette lou chief de la cainne en sa bouche, et cloie la bouche, si que li fumee n’en isse mie, mais viegne jusc’a la sansue;	Then pour the steam into it, and have the patient place their head end in their mouth, then seal their mouth so that no steam escapes but only goes up to the nostrils.
et la sansue cherra maintenant, et s’elle ne chiet, si rencomence la fumigation par maintes fois;	And now let the urine flow, and if it does not come, then start the fumigation repeatedly;
et soffre li malaides soif, et menjuce choses salees et als, et ne boive point d’aigue;	And let the patient endure thirst, and consume salty things and such, and do not drink any water;
et adonques li iert mestier qu’elle isse fuer par cest governement.	And then it's necessary for her to depart through this governance.
Et li forme de l’estrument a coi on trait la sansue, si est, quant on la puet veoir, semblans a tenailles corbés por mues entrer en la gorge;	And the shape of the tool used for the urine, when one can see it, resembles curved tongs to be inserted into the throat;
et ait semblance au bec de soigne, et i ait asperiteit de lime, si que ceu qu’elle prent, elle ne puet lassier;	And it has the appearance of a surgeon's hook, and it is rough like sandpaper, so that whatever she takes, she cannot leave it;
et vez ci la forme:	And here is the form:
li chapistres des apostemes	This chapter deals with abscesses.
Mout de semblances d’aposteme sont, selonc ceu que li remembrance vient ci aprés d’un et d’autre en cest livre, et sont diver en perforation et en taille;	No descriptions of pus exist, as per the recollection that comes after from one and another in this book, and they vary in puncturing and shaping;
