et c’est en II manieres dont l’une est en sa semblance meisme, et de ceu qu’il tient moistor.	And this is in two ways, one being in its appearance itself, and the other due to moisture.
Et li seconde maniere si est por les leus ou il sont au cors.	And the second way is for those limbs they are within the body.
car li apostemes dou chief est autres que cil dou fondement, et li apostemes dou leu charnut est autres que cil qui vient en jointures, et chescuns ait son jugement en l’uevre.	For the abscesses of the head are different from those in the foundation, and the abscesses of the internal body are different from those that come into joints, and each has its judgment in action.
Et si a apostemes c’on ne doit mie percier, tant que li bowe est meure selonc son acomplissement;	And if it's about abscesses, one should not prick them until the body has accomplished its completion according to its nature;
et si a de telz qu’il covient percier quant il sont crut, et ne meurent mie selonc lor acomplissement, si com aposteme qui sont delez jointures.	And for those that need to be pricked when they are formed, and do not die according to their completion, like abscesses located near joints.
Car quant apostemes vient delez jointures, et on le laisse tant qu’il est porris entor, par aventure si sont corrumput li liien et li nerf de la jointure, par coi ce est cause de contraction en celui membre.	And when abscesses are located at joints, and they remain swollen internally, by chance if the ligament and nerve of the joint have become corrupt, which is a cause of constriction in that limb.
Ou li aposteme est delez lou membre principel, et se tu tardes la perforation tant qu’il soit meurez, si nuira au membre principeil;	If the abscess is near the main member, and you delay the puncturing until it's fully formed, it will harm the main member.
ou il est delez lou fondement, si le perce on ainsois qu’il soit meurs;	If it is near the base, and you puncture it or do so as if it were fully formed;
et ne covient mie que tu perces aposteme crut sens digestion acomplie, fuers que celui qui est delez lou fondement, qu’il ne porrisse em parfont, et soit alongiez dedens, et i viegne fistule;	And it is not proper to puncture an abscess that has not been digested and fully completed its development, except for those located near the base, which might inflame internally and result in a permanent passage;
et ne puisse saner en grant termine.	And cannot heal thoroughly.
Et covient que tu saiches l’oure de la perforation de l’aposteme qui est meur selonc l’acomplissement, et c’est quant li dolor est apaisie, et li departemens de la fievre, et l’amenuisement de la dolor et de la roujor, et dou debatement et de l’aguisement dou chief de l’aposteme, et les autres signes;	And it is necessary that you know the time of the abscess perforation which occurs according to completion, and this is when the pain subsides, and the departure of the fever, and the reduction of the pain and redness, and the movement and hardening of the head of the abscess, and other signs;
et covient que tu faices seoir la perforation ou plus dependant leu de l’aposteme, et la ou il apert mues;	And it is necessary that you allow the perforation to occur where more depends of the abscess, and at which it opens.
et soit li perforation dou lonc dou cors, et se li apostemes est as mains ou as piez, ou en jointures et au ners et as arteres, et en toz leus igalz ou il n’a point de ploieure.	And let the perforation occur along the length of the course, and where it opens near the hands or feet, or at joints and necks and arteries, and everywhere else equally where there is no curvature.
En ces que ploient, par selonc celui membre.	In these cases, according to that member.
Et quant apostemes est en leu charnut, si vaut mues que tu laisses la perforation tant qu’il soit confermez en digestion acomplie, si com nos avons dit.	And when abscesses are in the fatty part of the body, it is right to wait until digestion has been completed before making an incision, as we have said.
Car se tu lou perces devant ceu, si iert alongiez li cors dou venim de lui, et est plains de mout d’ordure;	For if you pierce him in front of this, so that poison from his body flows out, and is full of little worms;
et par aventure endurcissent les levres et li parfondetez de lui.	and by chance harden the lips and deepen beneath him.
Et si a aucun aposteme que sont perciet selonc le large dou cors, selonc ceu que li membres en ait mestier.	And if in any abscesses they pierce according to the breadth of the body, as per what the body requires for its members.
Et covient que tu amenistres em petis apostemes, petis pertus;	And it is necessary that you take small pus-filled spots, small cuts;
et en grans apostemes, grans pertus, et maintes fendures selonc la semblance de la grandor de l’aposteme;	and in large pus-filled areas, large cuts, and many fissures according to the size of the pus area;
et si a de tels apostemes ou il covient chever lou keur, et coper;	and if there are such pus areas where it is necessary to clean out the wound and cover it.
quant il est jai devenus ausi com I drapelz, et est amortis, si covient faire ausi com on fait as bubes:	when it has become as white as linen and is healing, and when it has softened, you should do this as one does for boils:
et si a de telz que sont fendut en III angles, et si a de telz dont on cope ausi com la fuelle de mirte, si com apostemes des angres;	and if there are such that split into three corners, and those that one covers like the leaf of myrtle, like boils;
et si a de telz ou on fait une reonde taille, et autres tailles et semblant copeure.	And if such injuries or there is made a round cut, and other cuts and seeming to be cutting.
Cil qui n’ont point de chief, si com aposteme souef superficial, il covient que tu lou perces plainnement;	For those who lack a head, such as an abscess on the surface, it is necessary to pierce them thoroughly;
et covient quant li apostemes est gros, et il a coillit grant bowe, et tu lou perces, si ne traire mie toute la bowe en celle houre, mais en trai une partie;	And it is necessary when the abscesses are large and have formed a significant boil; if you pierce them, do not drain all the pus at once, but drain only part of it;
puis estoupe l’aposteme jusc’a l’autre jor, puis en trai aucune chose derechief;	Then let the abscess subside up to the other side, then leave no further treatment alone;
fai ceu par maintes fois de greit en greit, tant que li bowe isse toute;	Do this repeatedly from big to small, until all the pus has drained;
meismement se li malaides est de foible vertut, ou femme portans, ou petis enfes, ou viez hons decrepites.	Similarly, if the patient lacks strength, or is a woman in her pregnancy, or has young children, or elderly and feeble people.
Car li esperis tressaut aucune fois avec l’issue de la bowe, que par aventure muert li malaides, et tu ne t’en persois.	For when the attempt shakes every time with the expulsion of pus, perhaps causing death to the patient, and you do not notice it.
Eschuez donques cest chapistre par grant cautele, et quant tu as perciet ton aposteme, si essue la plaie, et regarde se li plaie de l’aposteme est petite;	Avoid this chapter with great caution, and when you have pierced the abscess, if there's an opening, observe if the wound from the abscess is small;
et se c’est une tailleure plainne, si amenistre tentes de lin ou de viez coton;	And if it's a flat cloth, you may use linen or wadded cotton to dress it;
et se c’est uns grans apostemes, et il i a mout de pertus, si covient que tu boutes en chescun une tente si qu’ele viegne l’une contre l’autre;	And if it's large abscesses with many perforations, you should make a tent in each one so that they will press against each other;
et se tu as copeit en l’aposteme une partie dou cuir, et tu l’as cheveit entor, si covient que tu l’emplisses de viel couton ou de rasure de dras de lin sens moistor, et le lie jusc’au tier jor;	And if you have cut through some of the skin in the abscess and sealed it internally, you should fill it with old cotton or linen thread debris without moisture, and tie it until midday;
puis l’oste, et le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then the meat, and treat with ointment as long as it is sound.
Et se decorremens de sanc avient a ton ovraige, si amenistre aigue froide et aisil, et moille I drapeil, et met sor le leu decorrant par maintes fois.	And if there is bleeding at your operation site, apply cold water gently and easily, and moisten the cloth, then place it on the affected area repeatedly.
Et se li decorremens de sanc persevere, se i amenistre governement et cure, et les poudres que j’ai dit em mains leus en cest livre, et se c’est ou tens d’iver, et li leus ou li apostemes est est mout nervous, si couvient que tu mettes sus tentes et drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile chaut;	And if the bleeding continues obstinately, you must apply government and treatment, and use the powders I have mentioned in this book for your hands. If it's or around a river, and either where your veins are or where your abscesses are is full of nervousness, then it should be that you put on moist tents and cloths soaked with wine and heated oil;
et se c’est en esteit, et li leus est charnus, si covient que tu mes sus drapelz moilliez en aigue et en oile, ou en vin et en oile froit, jusc’au tier jor, si com nos avons dit;	And if it's an internal issue and the patient is in flesh, then you should apply moist cloths with water and oil or wine and cold oil until the third day as we have said;
et puis deslie l’aposteme et l’essue et le cure, si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And then remove and clean the abscess, treating as it should be done, until it heals.
Et ceu covient il conoistre universement en cures des apostemes:	And it must be universally known in treatments of abscesses:
or vos ai dit coment on doit aler avant as cures des apostemes, et vez ci le chapistre.	Or you have been told how one should prepare before performing treatments for abscesses, and here is this chapter.
des soros	of the wounds
Ou keur dou chief vienent petis apostemes, et sont manieres de nous que sont en toiles, ausi com li josier d’une geline, et mout en i a de semblances.	Tiny abscesses come from the head, and they are in the form that we find them on cloths, like under a gooseberry's skin, and there are many that resemble these.
Il en i a de gras et de telz ou il a moistor ausi com poulz;	There are those with much moisture as well as those where there is moisture too, like in puddles;
et si a de telz qui sont dur et pierous au taillier, et n’i a point de doutance se li artere n’i fait contraire.	And there are those that are hard and stony to the surgeon's blade, and there is no doubt that it hits an artery and does not go against this.
Et li ovraiges de la taille si est que tu esprueve a tout I estrument qui est apelez «entromissoire», de coi li forme vient ci aprés, quel chose il contient.	And the procedures of cutting are such that you must test with all the instrument which is called "intromission", from which the following form comes, something it contains.
Car s’il contient moistor, si lou fent par desus dou lonc.	For if it contains moisture, if you make the incision too long.
Et quant li moistor est vuidie, si escorche sens rien laissier la peil qui contient celle moistor, car il revient adés quant on i laisse rien;	And when the moisture is drained, one scorches without leaving anything behind that contained this moisture, because it returns immediately once nothing is left.
puis plonge coton en oignement egiptien, s’il est presens;	then dip a cotton swab in Egyptian ointment if it's available;
se ceu non, en aigue et en seil, et en emple la plaie, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	if not that, in water and vinegar, and apply it to the wound, leaving it until the next day;
et ceu corront ceu qui est demorez dou nit.	And these concern those who are tormented by night.
Et pues rencomence lou coton, si com devant, le second jor, et lou tier, tant que tu saiches bien qu’il ne demoure point dou nit;	And continue with the cotton, just as before, on the second day and the third, until you are sure it does not last through the night;
puis cure la plaie d’oignement a ceu convenauble, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the wound with ointment as is suitable, until it heals.
Et se li apostemes tient I nout gras, si le cope selonc ceste forme, dou lonc;	And if the abscess holds its new fat content, shape it according to this form, along its length;
et i giete tes oncines, et l’escorche de toutes pars, et met toute ta cure de traire fuer la cotte ou il gist;	And pour your wounds, and apply the scorched parts from all sides, and place your entire treatment for bleeding in the coat where it lies;
et se li artere te fait contraire, si fai ceu que je t’ai dit aprés.	And if the artery does this differently, then do what I have told you after.
Et ausi fai de l’aposteme s’il est pierous, et dou taillier et dou curer si com je t’ai dit.	And similarly, treat if it's tubercular, and cut and cure as I have instructed you to.
Et li taille sus l’aposteme pierous et le moiste, si est plus legiere, car il sont de poc de sanc.	And when it comes to cutting on the tubercular abscess and moist area, it's easier because they contain less blood.
Et si a aucuns de ces apostemes ou chief ou il n’a point de moistor, et de ces fut I apostemes que je copai ou chief d’une vielle femme;	And if in any of these abscesses or heads there is no moisture, and of these newly formed abscesses that I made or came to be like a head of an old woman;
et trovai l’aposteme ausi com une piere xourde, aspre et blainche, et ne pooit brisier;	And I found the abscess as hard as a stone, rough and white, and it could not be broken;
et s’on en eust ferut aucun, on li eust ausi bien fait plaie com d’une piere.	And even if we had let out none of it, we would have made the wound as well just like with a stone.
En autres apostemes venans ou chief, fuer que ces qui vienent as chief des enfans et as racines des oreilles, li overture si soit toz jors au plus dependant leu, por mues issir la bowe;	In other abscesses coming or going from the head, those that come from the neck and the roots of ears, the incision should be as long as possible depending on its location, so that the pus may easily exit;
et les cure si com il covient.	And the treatment should be done accordingly.
des scrophules	regarding the treatment of scrophula
Maintes fois avienent cist aposteme au col, et desoz les asseles, et ens angres, et aucune fois vienent autre part ou cors, et sont mout, et sont enjanrees l’une avec l’autre.	Many times these abscesses occur at the neck, and around the armpits, and in the throat, and never come to any other part or corner, they are soft and are intertwined with each other.
Et chescune scrophule est proprement dedens sa cote, si com li nout et li aposteme dou chief, si com nos avons dit;	Each scrofula is properly within its bone, just like a nut and an abscess at the head, as we have said;
et les semblances de ces scrophules sont maintes.	And the appearances of these scrofulas are many.
Il i a de teles que contienent moistor, et si a de malignes qui ne vuellent obeir a santeit.	There are tele's that contain moisture, and some that don't want to comply with health.
en celle donques que tu vois de bone disposition au tochier, et est semblans a la color dou cors, et muet de chescune part et n’est mie aerse as ners dou col ne a l’artere ne au conduit, et n’est mie parfonde;	In this then, that you see in good position at the shoulder pit, and it resembles the color of flesh, and mute from each side and is not pressed under the collarbones nor around the artery or in the conduit, and is not deep;
si covient que tu la copes par desus, et l’escorche de chescune partie, et estent les II levres dou keur as oncines, se tu en as mestier, si com nos avons dit en apostemes dou chief;	It's necessary that you lift it from above, and scrape each part of it, and the two lips at the base should be exposed when needed, just like we have mentioned concerning abscesses in the head;
et la trai poc et poc, et soies seur que tu ne coper lou nerf ne la voine, et ne soit mie li spatumile agus ne trenchans, que li mains n’eschaipe, et ne voise trop avant, que tu ne coper mie ceu que tu ne dois.	Move it slowly and cautiously; make sure not to cut the nerve or the vein, nor let out too much pus but don't cut deeply either. Keep your hands steady and avoid cutting too far ahead, making sure you only cut what is necessary.
Et se tu copes la voinne ou l’artere, et ceu ne te laisse ovrer, si met en la plaie vitriole broiet, ou aucunes poudres que restainchent sanc, et estraint la plaie;	And if you cut the vein or artery and it does not allow you to open further, apply vitriol or any powders that stop blood flow into the wound, and restrain the bleeding;
et la laisse tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et soit amollie li plaie, et encomence a porrir.	And leave it until the abscess is soothed, and the wound becomes soft, and begins to rot.
Et quant li sans est estainchiez, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que tu l’acomplisses;	And when your blood is replenished, return to your task, until you complete it;
puis quier a ton doit indice s’il i demoure nules petites scrophules, si les cope et les munde.	Then follow your duty's sign if there remain any small warts, if you scrape and clean them.
Et s’il a en la racine de la scrophule voinne grant, si ne covient mie que tu copes celle scrophule en sa racine, mais la lie d’un fil double fort, et la laisse cheoir par li, sens nuisement;	And if there is a large vein at the root of the wart, it should not be that you scrape off that wart from its root, but tie it with a thick double thread and let it fall out by itself, without harm;
puis emple la plaie de viel coton plongiet en oignement egiptien, puis la cure.	Then apply old cotton soaked in Egyptian ointment to the wound, then proceed with the treatment.
Et se tu copes toute la scrophule, si covient que tu assembles les II levres de la plaie, et les cout maintenant, puis qu’il n’i a point demoreit de superfluiteit por la grandor de la scrophule.	And if you remove all the pimple, it is necessary that you join together the two lips of the wound, and stitch them now, then there should be no excess left due to the size of the pimple.
si covient que tu entendes a coper la racine de li, et traire fuer, et la cout si com nos avons dit.	And it is necessary that you cut to reach the root of it, and draw out pus, and stitch it as we have said.
Celles scrophules que tienent superfluiteit, perce lai ou il apert meure;	Those warts that occur due to excess, puncture where they appear if it is fatal;
et la perce ensi com celle devant dite, en dependant, puis i amenistre tentes avec oignement et semblans choses, si qu’elle corrompe ceu qui est demorez de la corruption;	And the puncture is done like the one before mentioned, in dependence, then he administers ointments and similar things with it, so that she (presumably referring to some medical treatment or substance) decays what has been left from the decay.
et quant li plaie est bien mundee, si la cure d’oignement enjanrant char, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when the wound is well cleaned, with ointment treatment encompassing flesh, as long as it remains clean.
de squinance	Regarding squint,
Li ancien dirent et parlerent de la tailleure de la gorge;	The old ones spoke and mentioned the surgery of the throat;
mais je ne vis onques en nostre terre qui la feist, et c’est li escripture de lor parole.	but I have never seen anyone perform it in our land, and that is their written word.
A ces qui ont squinance, il covient que li fendure de la gorge qui est apelee «epiglote» soit eschuee;	For those who have strabismus, it is necessary that the slit in the throat which is called "the epiglottis" be removed;
et c’on ne faice aide par ceu, por ceu que toutes les voines et li pormon dou malaide sont a ces qui ont aposteme chaut en la bouche, ou en la gorge ou en II amandres.	And it is not advisable to do this, because all the veins and the heart of the patient are close to those who have pus in their mouth, or in the throat, or in either lung.
Quant li maladie est en la chenal dou pormon, il covient coper l’epiglote por fuir la perdition qui vient de l’estranglement.	When the illness is within the channel of the lung, it is necessary to cover the epiglottis to prevent loss due to strangulation.
Il covient donques, quant nos volons fendre l’epiglote, que nos le fendons desoz III cercles ou IIII une petite fendure dou travers, entre les II cercles ou par la quantiteit de la fendure dou syfac, ne mie en la cartillaige;	Therefore, when we wish to cut the epiglottis, it should be cut through three circles or four with a small slit right across, between the second two circles. The size of this slit, according to its depth, not in the cartilage;
et cil leus si est covenaubles a la section de l’epiglote qu’il n’i a point de char, et li vasseil sont lonc d’enqui.	And if the lips allow for the division of the epiglottis there should be no fat, and the vessel is long outwards.
Et se li maistres est paourous, si covient qu’il estende le cuir de la gorge a tout l’oncine, puis fende lou keur tant qu’il viegne a la cheneil;	And if the surgeons are fearful, it is necessary for them to extend the throat skin throughout the inch, then cut into the bone until they reach the vein;
et eschue les vasselz de sanc, se tu vois aucune chose, et puis cope lou syfac, si com nos avons dit;	Avoid the blood vessels if you see nothing, and then expose the sinus, as we have said;
et est demostrez par la section dou fleume de la cheneil ki saut fuer par le leu qui est rompus, et par la defaute de la voix;	And demonstrated by the section of the windpipe that leaps out through the limb that is broken, and by the loss of voice;
et laisse la plaie overte une piece.	Let the wound remain open for a space.
Et quant li houre est passee de coi on doute l’estranglement, assemble les II levres de la plaie dou keur, et la cout toute soule sens la cartillaige;	And when the time has passed during which one doubts strangulation, gather the two edges of the wound neatly together, and sew all smoothly without the cartilage;
puis aministre medicines qui font naistre char, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then administer medicines that promote flesh growth, as long as it is sound.
Albucasim dist c’on ne faice ce jusc’a tant que li gorge est toute estoupee, et li malaides est jugiez a mort, et li defaut li alaine.	Albucasim, instruct that this should be done until the throat is completely swollen, and the patient's life judged to be at an end, and when there is no further improvement.
Adonques cope on l’epiglote por ceu que li malaides ne puet alener, et il respire par la plaie, et ensi est gardez de mort;	Then operate the epiglottis because the patient cannot breathe properly, and they inhale through the wound, and thus you prevent death;
et por ce commanderent li anciain a laissier la plaie overte tant que li malice de la maladie soit passee, et elle est passee en III jors ou en IIII Et adonques il comanderent a coudre la plaie et curer, tant qu’elle fut curee;	And to command the old ones to leave the wound open until the disease's illness passes, and it has passed after three or four days, and then they commanded to stitch up the wound and clean it, as long as it was being cleaned;
et je vos dirai ceu que je vis.	And I will tell you what I have seen.
Je vis que une damoisele prist I coutel, et le ficha en sa gorge, et copa partie des chenelz dou pormon;	I see that a maiden took an iron knife and stabbed it into her throat, cutting parts of the windpipe.
et je fui apelez por li curer, et la trovai ausi com morte.	And I was called to treat her, and found her just as dead.
Je descovris la plaie, et trovai le sanc qui en estoit issus, et soi bien qu’elle n’avoit mie copeit voine ne conduit fuer que la gorge, et li vens issoit fuer par la plaie.	I discovered the wound and found the blood that was issuing from it, and indeed, it wasn't accompanied by a severed artery or exit route other than the throat, and the veins bled through the wound.
Je me hastai, et cousi la plaie, et la curai tant qu’elle fut sanee;	I hurriedly treated the wound, and after she was healed, I cured it.
et n’avint a la damoisele fuer qu’elle fut roge de voix, et revint aprés a sa disposition;	And the maiden spoke with difficulty for days and eventually returned to her usual state of health.
por ceu di je que en la tailleure de l’epiglote n’ait mie paour.	Therefore, I say that in the surgery of removing the epiglottis, one should take care not to harm it.
de la grosse gorge	In the large throat
Cist apostemes est apelez «hernie de gorge», et est uns grans apostemes en color d’une jaisse, et est molt en femmes;	These abscesses are called "neck hernias," and they are large, dark-colored abscesses that occur frequently in women.
et est selonc II manieres:	And there are according to two manners:
naturez, et accidens;	natures, and accidents;
ou natureil n’a point d’engien.	or natural has no disease.
Et li accidens est selonc II manieres, de coi l’une est semblans a gras nous, et li autre maniere est semblans a aposteme qui vient de nous d’artere;	And the accidents occur in two ways, of which one resembles that coming from us, and the other way resembles an abscess that comes from our veins;
et il i ait paour, et ne covient mie ovrer de feir fuers que en celi qui est petite, et le prueve et cerche a tout l’intromissoire:	and there is fear, and it should not have any cuts made except in those who are small, and the proof and search extend to every intervention:
se tu le trueves ausi com I nout gras, et ne pent a nulle voine, si le cope, si com on cope les nous, et le trai a tout sa coife, s’il en i a point;	if you find it as soft as the back of our hands and cannot puncture any vein, then operate, just like we operate on our hands, and treat every part completely, if there is even a hint of disease.
et encerche bien tot, et le cure si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	And search thoroughly then, and treat it as is appropriate, until it is healed perfectly.
des nous	from the bones
Maintes manieres de nous sont, dont je dirai toutes les semblances;	Many ways there are for us, of which I will mention all the similarities;
et or covient que je die toute la difference qui est entre nout et issue.	And it is fitting that I should mention all the differences that exist between us and them.
Je dis que issue est chalors et fievre tenans, tant que li ebulicions est passee, et est acomplie li porriture;	I say that in the case of an infection and fever, until the body's eruptions have subsided, and after completion of the putrefaction;
adonques repose li fievre et li chalor.	Then the fever and heat subside.
Avec lou nout n’a ne chalor ne fievre ne dolor, et contient I syfac, qui est ses propres sac et est selonc la color dou cors, et encomence ausi com une jaisse, et devient gros;	In the case of us, there is no heat, fever or pain, and contains its own sack, which is akin to the flesh's cavity and starts out similarly as a gooseberry, and grows in size;
et sont selonc II semblances, ou grais, ou moiste, et mout de color sont si com j’ai dit en la division.	And they are according to two appearances, or greasy, or moist, and little color as I have said in the division.
Il covient, quant tu viens a la cure dou nout, que tu esprueves et l’enquier premierement a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «entromissoire», selonc ce que sa forme venra ou chapistre qui est aprés.	When you come to the treatment of new injuries, it is necessary that you first inspect and inquire about all the tool which is called 'the adjuster', according to its shape or chapter that follows.
Et li maniere de l’inquisicion des apostemes des nous est que tu preignes ou plus moiste leu que tu trueves en l’aposteme, et torne tes dois poc et poc, tant que tu saiches que li estrumens ait perciet le keur, puis que ce soit selonc la grandor de l’aposteme;	And the method of incising abscesses is that you take or find the more moistened part than you find in the abscess, and turn your fingers a little bit by little bit, until you know that the instruments have pierced the pus, then according to the size of the abscess;
puis estrai l’entromissoire, et pren garde en ceu que saut fuer.	Then extract the pus, and be careful not for it to jump out.
Se moistor corrans cort, queil color elle ait, si le fent si com j’ai dit des autres apostemes;	If moisture is running down, whatever its color may be, cut it in the same way as I have said for other abscesses;
et se aprés l’entromissoire nen vient moistor, saiches qu’il est gras, si le fent donques en croix, et le prent as pinceures, et l’escorche legierement de chescune part et warde la cotte ou il gist que tu la traies saine avec le nout;	And if no pus comes out after the pus, you know it's greasy, then cut it in a cross shape, and hold it with tweezers, and gently burn each side from every part; guard the place where it lies that you may pull out the grease alive with the rest.
et se tu ne la pues traire saine, si la trai par pieces si qu’il n’i demoure rien.	And if you cannot bring it whole, take it piece by piece so that nothing remains.
Car s’il i demoure rien, si revient li nous par maintes fois;	For if there is nothing left, the body will come back through many times;
et s’il en demore un poc, et li sans te grieve, si emple la plaie d’aucunes poudres corrosives agues, et estraint la plaie, et met sus choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if there is a little left, and it does not trouble you, use powders that are corrosive and wet for the wound, restrain the wound, apply things that soothe abscesses heated, and treat it with other treatments until it is whole;
et se li nous est grans, si cout les II levres de la plaie, et le cure de ceu qui enjanre char.	And if the wound is large, cut the two lips of the wound, and treat in this manner what needs to be done with what is injured flesh.
et se li voine batans t’est contraire ou autre si te haste et emple le leu de vitriole broiet, et lou laisse liiet II jors ou III, tant que li plaie porrisse, et repose li ebulicion dou sanc;	And if the vein is too large or another way you hurry, use the inside of a roasted grape peel and let it lie for two or three days, until the wound cooks, and rest with blood boiling;
puis revien au coper ceu que i est demoreit dou nout.	Then return to observe what has been delayed by the newness of it.
Vez ci les formes des estrumens entromissoires, et sont de III manieres:	Here are the forms of the interstitial organs, and they are in three ways:
grans et moien et petit;	large, medium, and small;
et s’en i a III quarrez qui sont apelez «albaret», et I qui est apelez «breb», et s’en i a de III manieres:	and there are three pairs of them, which are called "albaret," and one is called "breb," and they come in three ways:
grant, moien, et petit, por encerchier les apostemes de fistule;	large, medium, and small, to encompass the abscesses of fistulas;
et sont ausi com les aguilles dont on cout les sorceles, et sont d’arain citrin, ou de fer, ou d’argent, et mues valent cil qui sont jaune, et sont plus esprovez de plonc noir por encerchier les corbeures de fistule;	and they are also like needles that one uses to cut the roots, and they can be of carnelian, or iron, or silver, and golden ones are considered better for cutting away at the swellings of fistulas;
et sont de III manieres:	And there are three ways:
grans, moiens, et petis, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce des pertus.	Large, medium, and small, according to the size of the width of the defects.
Les formes des oncines sont de mout de semblances, si com tu vois ci:	The shapes of the horns resemble sheep, as you see here:
grans, moiens, et petis;	large, medium, and small;
et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures de III manieres ausi;	and for horns that have two curves in three ways;
et si a oncines qui ont III corbeures, et sont ausi de III manieres;	and for horns with three curves, they also occur in three ways;
et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures, et oncines d’une corbeure soulement, et sont de III manieres;	and for horns that have two curves, and horns with just one curve, they also occur in three ways;
et tuit cist sont necessaire en lor leu.	And all this must be considered in their location.
Li chief de ces a coi on fent sont trenchant, et de telz i a qui ne taillent mie fuer que d’une part, dont on escorche les nous, por ceu c’on ne cope la voine ne le nerf;	The tip of this is to be sharp, and for some it does not cut fully but only from one side, which we shave because there is no vein or nerve;
et de ces intromissoires sont les alemeles reponues en mainches, si que li malaide ne s’en persoivent a l’overture des apostemes;	And these interventions are answered with responses placed in gloves, so that the patient does not notice them during the opening of abscesses;
et sont de III manieres:	and there are three ways:
grant, petit, et moien, si com tu vois;	greatly, little, and moderately, as you see;
et n’en use on mie fuer que en leu charnut, si com jambes, et bras, et mameles, et as angres, et en semblans leus;	and one uses none of them except in the sensitive parts such as legs, arms, nipples, and bones, and similarly to these;
et aucune fois fait on I autre estrument petit, semblant a escorces de fistices, selonc ceste forme, a coi on estainche sanc:	and no other small tool resembling whips' thongs is ever used according to this form, to which bleeding is stopped:
et le met on aucune fois au leu qui saine a copement des voines, et as arteres, et aucune fois reont selonc ceste grant forme:	And it is placed in the healthy part of the body, at the junctions of veins and arteries, and never according to this large form:
Aucune fois enflent les mameles d’aucuns homes quant cil encomencent estre corrumput, tant qu’eles semblent mameles de feme;	None of the men's nipples swell until they seem like women's nipples when they begin to become corrupt;
et demorent laides et enflees, et qui les vuet curer, si le covient soier selonc ceste forme des ceste ligne .b. jusques a .g.:	And remain deformed and swollen, and those who wish to cure them should treat according to this form of this line .b. until .g.:
puis escorche la graisse, et emple la plaie de medicine enjanrant char, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie a costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	Then scrape off the fat, and apply medicine to promote healing on the wound. Sew together the two edges of the wound, and continue treatment until it heals;
et se li mamele cline aval, et est amolie por sa grandor si com il avient as femmes, si la fent en II costelz desus, par II semblans fendures;	And if the mammary gland is deformed downwards and is flattened due to its size, like it appears in women, if she cuts it into two pieces above, by two similar slits;
de coi l’une soit tenans a l’autre a la fin de l’une et de l’autre, si que li plus grans ligne conteigne la menor selonc ceste forme, des ceste ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.;	Due to which the larger line contains the smaller one until both ends at last, so that this pattern follows according to this form, from this line .b. up to this line .g.;
puis escorche le cuir qui est entre les II levres, et oste la graisse, et i amenistre ceu que nos avons dit de costure et de poudres, et ceu qui est necessaire en la cure, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then scrape off the skin that is between the two edges and remove the fat. Apply what we have instructed about sewing and powders, as well as anything necessary for treatment until it heals;
et s’il n’est sanez, ou li incision n’est mie toute faite, por ceu que li malaides ne vuet reposer, ou por le decorrement de sanc, si covient que tu emplisses la plaie de coton moilliet en oignement corrosif;	And if it is not healed, or the incision has not been fully completed, because the patient does not wish to rest, or due to bleeding, it is necessary that you fill the wound with moist cotton in corrosive ointment;
et le laisse tant qu’il menjuce le remenant et la graisse, puis le cure tant qu’il soit saneis.	And leave it until it starts to heal, by adjusting and massaging the wound with fat, then continue treating it until it has healed completely.
des apostemes des asselles	from abscesses of the armpits
Cist apostemes que vienent desoz les asseles sont manieres de scrophules dures ou il ait cotes, et s’en i a que contienent moistor.	Abscesses that originate in the armpits are manners of hard scrofulas where there are nodes, and if there are any containing moisture.
Cil donques qui contienent moistor covient qu’il soient copez selonc ceste forme, des la ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.:	Those who contain moisture should have their limbs cut according to this form, from the line .b. up to the line .g.:
Et quant toute li bowe qui est en l’aposteme est vuidie, si emple la plaie de viel coton, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor, puis oste tout le coton, et cure d’oignement avenant a ceu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when all the pus in the abscess has drained out, fill the wound with old cotton and let it be for another day, then remove all the cotton, and apply ointment until it is healed.
Et se li apostemes est de semblances de scrophules, si le fent si com nos avons dit en fendures des scrophules, et se li plaie rent bowe, si amenistre cautere si com nos avons dit devant.	And if the abscesses resemble scrofula sores, make incisions as we have said in cuts for scrofula sores, and if the wound is filled with pus, apply a cautery as we have said previously.
de la routure de l’artere	regarding the rupture of an artery
Quant li artere est route, et li cuir est soudez qui est sus, si en vient maintes fois apostemes, et tout aussi avient il a la voine enflee et aposteme;	When the artery is cut and skin is stitched above it, many times abscesses form, and similarly, this occurs with a punctured vein and abscess.
et si le conoist on ensi quant c’est por l’artere, si est li apostemes lons em parfont;	And if one knows that for the artery, such abscesses extend fully inwards;
et quant tu le sens a tes dois, si sens I estraignement;	And when you feel it with your fingers, if you sense the constriction;
et quant c’est por la voine, si est reons defuer aparans;	And when it's due to a vein, reasons of escape are apparent;
et c’est folie de coper cest aposteme, et meismement quant il est desoz les asseles et as angres et ou col et em mout d’autres leus, et est mout grans.	And it's madness to deal with this abscess, and similarly when there are boils and sores and in the neck or under other things, and they are very large.
Il covient donques eschuir la cure de fer, et celui qui est a chief covient eschuir ausi, et en celui qui est d’enfleure d’artere fent par desus le cuir dou lonc;	So it is necessary to avoid the iron treatment. One who has a head wound should also avoid this, and in the one who is inflamed by an artery, do so above the skin for as long;
puis oevre la taille as oncines, et depart bellement l’artere des toiles, tant qu’ele soit descoverte;	Then work in small sections, and beautifully remove the artery from the tissues, until it is exposed;
puis boute desoz li une aguille, et la fai percier jusc’a l’autre costeit, et estraint l’artere d’un fil double en II leus, selonc ceu que je t’ai ensigniet en l’estraction des II arteres qui sont en temples;	Then stick inside one thread, and make it pierce to the other side, and bind the artery with a doubled string for two loops, just like what I taught you in removing the arteries that are in the temples;
puis point le leu qui est entre les II liens d’un intromissoire tant que li sans en isse qui i est, et soit deliiez li aposteme;	Then take the limb which is between the two loops of an introducer until the pus which is inside is released and thereby relieve the abscess;
puis amenistre la cure que enjanre bowe, tant que li liien chient;	Then administer the treatment that irritates the wound, as long as the thread enters.
puis cure ceu d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat this with ointment, as long as it is clean;
et se li apostemes est por la taille de la voinne, si covient que tu teignes a ta main ceu que tu pues de l’aposteme a tout le cuir, puis boute l’aguille desoz le leu que tu tiens a ta main, et la fai percier, et i ait I fil double, si que tu le trais de l’autre costeit;	And if the abscess is due to the size of the vein, it is necessary that you color your hand with what you can of the pus all over the skin. Then pinch out the needle from your held limb, and pierce it, and place two threads, so that you lead them from the other side;
puis lie l’aposteme, si com je t’ai dit, ou liien de l’une de II pars as II chiés dou fil;	Then tie the pus or vein, just as I told you, or one part of the two shoulders with the thread;
et se tu doutes que li filz n’isse fuer, si i reboute une autre aguille a tout I fil desoz tout l’aposteme a l’incision de la premiere aguille, et estraint les filz en IIII leus;	And if you doubt that the child will survive, should you replace another needle with all its thread over the entire abscess at the incision of the first needle, and hold the threads in four places;
puis cope l’aposteme tant que li superfluitez en isse, puis cope la superfluiteit dou keur et laisse ceu qui est liiez;	Then remove the abscess as long as there's excess, then remove the excess slowly and leave what is tied;
puis met sus I drapeil moilliet en vin et en oile, puis li amenistre cures de tentes et d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then place on the bandage a moistened cloth in wine and oil, then apply treatments of poultices and ointments until they are healed.
des apostemes des ners	Of abscesses of nerves
Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.	Also like abscesses appearing in arteries and veins, they appear on nerves when they are cut or due to too much work, and similar things.
Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor;	This happens more often with shoulders and elbows and in all places where joints are, and this is the symptom of abscesses, and its color resembles the color of flesh, and it can be found in various positions without pain;
et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur;	And when one restrains it in form, the patient feels pain, and is not completely satisfied by its harmony with the body, but over the heart;
et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer:	And moves in all directions, neither forward nor backward, nor to the side or above, and that which is in joints does not fit well when covered with iron:
par aventure i vanroit contraction;	By chance it would result in tightening;
et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.	And that which is on the head or forehead causes the skin to become inflamed.
Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine;	If it's an abscess and small, if you have tweezers, then grip it at its root;
et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If it's large, lift it at the spine, and scrape, then cut into the bone, and stitch the wound together when it heals completely, and treat until there is no pain.
des grosses boces pendans	Of large boils hanging down
Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros;	No disease happens in wombs or anywhere else in this way, and it is a sickness that is called "fungus" by its appearance, and has subtle roots, and the knots are large;
et en i a de petis et de mout grans;	and there are both small and quite large ones;
et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	And I saw someone who had two or three in their abdomen that were more like fungi than anything else, and there was no difference, they were white, had small roots, and were cracked, and corrosion occurred right away with moisture.
Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine;	I copied them and found that in one, it weighed XVIII ounces, and in the other VI З., and when you look at the incisions during surgery, if you see that the muscles are moist, and the color of the artery is white and moist with a subtle root;

puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres;	then let the blood flow gradually, as it is natural;
et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And put powder on and over the powder I apply glue of a half-cooked egg yolk mixed with rose water, stewed with oil rosy and fresh, and leave it until the next day, then continue to treat with other treatments as long as they are cured.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:	The formation of forces in the universe is like this:
li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	Let the two shoulders be in harmony and cut them equally, and let the shoulders also be as large as the arms evenly:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;	The error in creation happens when the kidneys escape during incision;
donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	Therefore, you should extend it to your nail so that the blood will form an abscess;
et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	And shape it evenly, and if you cannot hold it at your nail, then keep it with pliers, and then shape it.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;	And if they penetrate for three days, and the one who is in the middle of the penis swells, if he leaves them until the abscesses have subsided, and gently scorch him.
si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	And if he can withstand it like you can bear it, and keeps the part of the penis away from him, it won't harm him at all.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;	So treat the area of sudden wounds with powder, as we have said or treated with powders, and if you endure a little more heat, it won't cause any harm;
cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Treat accordingly, as we have said, while he remains healthy.
dou retenement de l’urine	The retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	Retaining urine is due to obstruction by stone or blood clotting, or bowel obstruction, or a dead fetus, or similar things that we have mentioned in the section;
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	And if his urine is not flowing, and you see there's retention due to a stone in the bladder or neck of the bladder, it must be that the patient should be made to squat.
et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet;	And have his feet placed on the back, and extend his belly from the part above the back, and restrain the patient so he bends as much as he can.
et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	And then the neck of the bladder is forced to express the stone above, so that the urine starts flowing again.
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme:	And if it doesn't come out, as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you should administer an extraction with all the instrument called "syringe", which has this form:
et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil;	And may it be made of fine silver wire, like the feathers of a bird;
et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	And let the length of the cane be one palm and a half long, and be slender at its tip.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;	And the method for directing urine flow involves taking a double thread, and attaching it to the small end of the fabric or cotton, then threading the fabric inside the syringe.
et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	and cut off the excess of the fabric and insert it up to the tip of the syringe, then grease the syringe with oil or butter and egg yolk, and have the patient sit on a chair, and massage the bladder and penis with wet oil and olive oil.
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;	then gently place the syringe in the penis, until it reaches the base of the penis, then bend the penis upwards towards the tip.
puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;	Then push the syringe ahead until it reaches the bladder, and let the patient feel the sensation going up to the empty thing, and this is not done exactly as ordered because for him who led her where she was going, she was twisted.
puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	Then stretch the thread all the way with a gentle tug, and let the urine follow the thread, then pull it out gently, making sure to properly drain the urine.
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	And continue with the syringe until the bladder is emptied, and ensure that the patient feels the sensation of emptying.
des maladies de la vessie	Concerning diseases of the bladder
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When burns or blood come into the bladder, or putrefaction gathers there, and you see distilled waters and medicines, if make everything to the instrument that is called 'clepsis', and this is its form:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus:	It's sealed, and if it has been closed for three days:
II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	Two on one side, and one on the other, as you see;
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	And let the legs be positioned where the medicine could correctly affect the penis without adding to its sensation. If moisture can be removed, drain it when necessary;
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	And when you see your medicine flowing into the bladder, place the patient under moisture and guide him to the one who is doing it.
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	Then drain the moisture with the knife, and afterwards firmly set the guide in place;
si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	If the moisture enters inside now, and reaches the bladder, so that the patient feels it;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:	And this is the form of the subtle colic where one irrigates the bladder:
si est ci:	Here it is:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	And can be made of silver or lead, and the shoulder joint is higher up;
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	And down to the breast or to the joints of the shoulder;
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	Then take a sheep's bladder and fill it with the moisture that you are going to irrigate the bladder with, then tie it between the two breasts using a good strong double thread, and heat one end of this moisture on fire;
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	Then apply a potion to the head of the bladder in the penis, then hold your hand over the bladder until all moisture is present, as long as the patient feels that this moisture has reached the bladder;
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;	And if you do not have a bladder, take a piece of parchment and make it into a circle, then pierce it smoothly around.
puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	Then thread a strong string through these holes, then join the circle like one would join a loop, and place inside what you see of moisture and water and steam, and tie it with the tool.
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	And do this like you did for the bladder, pressing with your hand until the moisture reaches the bladder.
de la piere	of the stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	We have spoken about the methods of stone extraction and combination of medicines in this section.
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	And I have explained the difference between a kidney stone that is wet and another, and all the signs, and in which kidney one should operate with size;
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	And in the bladder, and in the penis;
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	And I will explain it to you clearly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	I say that the stone in the bladder often occurs more frequently in children, and this is a sign that there is an obstruction of the bladder like an obstruction in its subtlety;
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	And at the urethra opening, and massage the patient's penis, and let it harden many times, and then return to its original state;
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	and in these cases of obstruction there is a base;
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	and the healing is lighter for children until they are four years old, and becomes more painful in elderly individuals, and it's somewhere between childhood sicknesses and aging conditions;
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	And it is easier to treat those with large stones than those with small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to treatment, it is first necessary to cleanse the patient by laxation, in order to remove all the bile that is within the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	Because it clogs up every time when trying to cut into the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	Then take hold of the patient by their limbs, and lift and move them downward, so that the stone descends into the bladder and comes out only once below their waist;
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	then have them sit between your hands, with their hands on their thighs, so that the bladder is fully tilted downward;
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	then inquire and touch inside;
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	if you feel the stone in space, then hurry to cut on the stone now.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	And if she doesn't urinate upon touching her whole length, moisten your index finger of the left hand with oil, for if the patient is female; or your middle finger, if the patient is young and mature.
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	And place it at its base, hold the stone, and when you feel it with your finger, if it moves in the neck of the bladder;
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	Then press with your finger, and push the stone outward where you see to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	And instruct the surgeon to press the bladder with his hand, and command him to spread his right hand upwards over the kidneys, and use his left hand to stretch the skin beneath the kidneys in the area where the cut will be made;
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	Then take out the mucus-filled stone, which has this shape:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	And make the incision between what is between the kidneys and the base, not in the middle but at the edge of the left lung;
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	And be straight on the stone, and your hands either on edge or foundation, and be tied such that it passes through, and is wide outside but narrow inside, according to the size of the stone, not too large;
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	By chance if the press is made on the base or foundation, it might leap as though it were doing its own work;
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	Know that there may be stone parts with corners and edges:
si est griés a issir;	If it is strained to exit;
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	And if it's on parts below, resembling a thorn and round, from which the exit is light.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	Above, where there are corners and edges, make the size larger;
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	And if it does not jump, then you should pull with the tongs that are like a file at their tip, to force the stone so it doesn't escape;
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	For you should use a sharp curved instrument to remove from beneath the head;
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	And if you cannot use it like that, if it's large or small and blunt, and if it doesn't have a smooth surface, then coat it with vitriol;
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	And if there are more than one stone, remove the larger one first from the neck of the bladder, then proceed upwards, then pull it down forcefully, and after that, remove any smaller ones if there are more.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if she is very large, then it would suit to let her out, and make a larger wound.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	For two things happen to the patient:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	or he dies, or his urine comes out immediately when his kidneys cannot join;
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	but try to do it with the forceps, or using them as pincers, until you pull it out piece by piece;
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	And when you have completed your work, apply the incision with frankincense and aloes and dragon's blood, compress it, and place above it a wad of moist cloth in oil and wine, or in oil and rose water and cold water, to soothe the inflamed wound;
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	Then bind the hair on its neck, and don't untie the knot until three days.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you remove the bandage, wash it thoroughly with water and wine vinegar, then apply a diaper ointment and basil ointment until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	And if abscesses occur in the wound and blood congeals in the bladder, and is kept there by this means, causing retention of urine, which is known to do so that without jumping with urine:
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	So burn in the wound, and remove that blood, for if it remains, it will inflame the bladder, and damage it;
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then cleanse the wound from water, pus, and scum, and assist in all manners that you find, until it becomes clean.
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	And it is necessary that when you treat all the wounds, you tie both legs together and apply the remedies to the body.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	And if the stone is small, and it comes from the penis, being lodged inside, and cannot allow urine to pass;
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	If you treat as I have instructed, cut him many times, and forgive the loss caused by this treatment.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I already know this experience like this.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	Take one iron branch according to this form, and have it pierced at three points on each side.
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	Then take a thread and tie it around the penis near the stone, so that it cannot come back into the bladder;
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	Then cut in the penis lightly until you reach the stone;
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	And turn the drill with your hand in the stone little by little, until you can penetrate the stone from another side;
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	If it comes quickly, then press your hand on the one that is stuck inside the stone which is within the penis.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	If it breaks soon, and jump with urine, and the patient will feel relief;
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	And if you cannot do this for any reason that obstructs it, tie one thread around the stone and the other over it, then place the penis between the two threads, then force him out, and untie the thread, and cleanse the congealed blood that is in the wound;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And treat it as long as there is bleeding.
de la piere des femmes	From the stone of women
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	A situation arises where a stone might be found in women, and when it happens even once, the treatment is difficult, and is forbidden for three reasons:
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	One reason is that perhaps the woman is still a virgin;
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	The second reason is that one cannot know who is naked even when she is modest, even if she is pure.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	And the third way is that perhaps one cannot find a woman well knowing this art of hands;
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	And the fourth way is that the stone of the woman might be larger in circumference than the stone of a man, so it requires deeper cutting and great fear. If necessity leads to this, then you should seek out someone very skilled, and lead them to see where you are, and if you don't find a suitable place there, not even from a modest woman.
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	And it addresses a fine task in the life of women, where a woman who understands part of the art, and is commanded to do what you command about the incision into the stone;
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	and carefully consider if that woman is a virgin:
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	therefore, she must push her desire or foundation and seek the stone;
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	and if she finds it, make her follow the path or direction of her desire and seek the stone; I advise her to push with all her strength or power under her desire in the body, and press and urge her left hand against the bladder in its form.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	And if she finds it, it's necessary that she move it from side to side as she enters the bladder until under, as long as she comes to the root of the thigh;
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	Then cut on the stone near the root of the thigh in the middle of the bone, right where muscles are attached, and feel the stone in that area.
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	and don't move his hands near the stone or beneath it, and cut him at the head first with a small incision.
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	then open the incision to the head, if you feel the stone increase the wound as long as the stone can come out forcefully, and know that many types of stones exist:
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	This is to say, there are small and large ones, rough and smooth, long and round, and that they have corners.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	If you understand the signs to know the outcome.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if it doesn't hurt you, put lime water on it and keep it there for an hour until the pain subsides;
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	Continue with your work, as long as the stone is strong, and have at hand the tools I told you about for extracting stones in your home to assist you in your task.
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	And if it does not weaken you, and it's an artery that has been cut, apply the powder to the site and hold firmly with threads or strips, and do not repeat this procedure. Leave the stone alone and don't try to extract it, in case the patient might die.
puis cure la plaie.	Then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood has calmed down and the limbs are restored, then return to your work while the stone is hard.
de hernie carnouse	of fatty hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	Rice in water is nothing else but a mixture of moisture or white slime, which resides under the skin that contains an egg;
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	And it is called "slime," and in no case is it truly within the egg membrane if one considers that it might be another egg;
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	And this is the skin between the white fat, as we have said;
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	And that does not have that pit.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the formation of this gelatinous growth is due to weakness that affects the kidneys, and spreads that substance.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	And whenever there is percussive impact on the testicles, and this moisture has many colors:
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	or it turns yellow like jaundice, or it lacks redness, or is black, or watery white, and this happens more often;
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	and these are the signs to recognize this assemblage, for if it is white like what we have said, then it indicates pus, and its length is similar to that of an egg, and does not protrude from the testicles, because there is moisture all around.

Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	So, I say that the art of restraint is done in two ways:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	One way is through attraction, or through creating an opening.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	In the method of using attraction, we make the animal sit in hot water until its horns soften and during that time;
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	Then take hold of it with your hands, until they are healed and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille:	For the tail correction:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	It is necessary that you dye the beast and press its flanks with your left hand. et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	and let no wound or subtle wound exist under the vesicles;

puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	Then treat the wound until it has healed.
des hermofrodites	Regarding hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	Hermaphroditism occurs in two ways at home:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	One way is when between the two genitals opening as in the natural figure of a woman, or having hair, and sometimes passing urine.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	The other way is for women, having at the wrist like a penis and two openings.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	And the treatment for fever and illness is such that you treat all the joints properly, and the healing process like other wounds;
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	In the second way, for men whose urine jumps through the skin of the kidneys, if there is no treatment.
de la tentigene	From the scab or soreness
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	A tenting joint is an improperly placed joint in the natural part, as long as it looks too ugly to see;
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	And some women have it as large as a hand, and this is the treatment.

de erratique	Regarding the irregularity
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	Erratic if the essence of the female is not understood, or if the parts are small;
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	And is natural by birth, or accidental due to illness that has come about;

des emorroides	Of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Thromboses are openings of veins where without proper care, and when thromboses become old they turn into varicose.

de l’enfantement	Of childbirth
