si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	Do it according to what is proper.
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you treat the woman who has lost her dead child or whose abdomen is affected, as I have explained in the division section, and if it doesn't come out, then you are forced to intervene with your hands.
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	It is necessary for you to know if she possesses sound virtue, and if she has not experienced any accidents or fears of death;
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	It is necessary for the woman to be attentive on her back, and have her shoulders tilted forward, and her legs lifted;
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	And let the minister prepare in two parts, or bind her to the bed so that she is not treated during the descent of the child;
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	Then rub the lips of the pregnant woman with moist olive oil using a mixture of rosemary and fenugreek seeds and flaxseed, then smear her hands with these oils and spices;
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	Then let her move lightly on the pregnant woman, then place her in a position where she can easily move her hips, and prepare to ensure that when the child descends through her head;
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	If the hairs are stuck in his eyes or neck or mouth or palate or under the beard or on the collarbone or near the ribs, and if he descends into stones, then they should be pricked or pierced near the middle of the back.
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	And it is necessary that you cut the hair with your right hand, and place the bend between his fingers of his left hand, and he pushes him with all his hand lightly, and insert the hair into none of these parts that we have mentioned, until it reaches the empty thing.
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	And this is the form of the hair:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	Then insert against another hair, or the third if necessary, so that the extractions may be equal;
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	And then extend them equally by moving on one side and the other, to facilitate extraction, and make sure that the hairs are toothed for holding during extraction, as this is how it should be done:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if there remains a part of it, let someone oil some of its skin from elsewhere, and place it on that part, and draw out the other part.
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	And if there remains nothing at all, place this onion or higher up the body, and do this until it exits completely.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes before the other, and it cannot be pulled back due to being squeezed, then you must wrap around the first, until it exits completely;
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	Then apply the paste at the joint of the sole or in the crease, and similarly do this with the other hand, and for both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the child's head is large and it becomes obstructed during delivery, or if its forehead is assembled with sharpness, then you should puncture the bony spatule with your fingers and make the forehead and remove the sharpness;
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	For you will find it in the instrument which is called 'almidach', whose shape comes with the instruments or chapter that follows this one.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and thus let them pass naturally at birth by the same means;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and then pull the bones with tongs, and if it breaks and is held by force until it splits, as long as the moisture or worse comes out;
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if it cannot come out, then cut it piece by piece according to what you can do;
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	and if it is swollen in the belly or under the ribs, you must let it out as long as the moisture flows.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the fetus is on its feet, there is a slight attraction, and the movement to the mouth of the birth canal is also slight.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is stuck in the belly or under the buttocks, you must extract it through the skin that covers the hand.
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	And they perform on the belly or the buttocks wherever there is moisture present;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	And if the other bones are affected by osteitis and the shoulder remains dislocated, he takes hold of his patient's arm up to the elbow joint, and guides it until it reaches the opening in the joint.
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	Then he performs either the first or second method, and forces him to move;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	And if the opening in the joint is narrowed due to an abscess that has formed, it is not suitable for manual labor; rather, it should be treated with moist and greasy substances.
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	And the patient is administered plaster, and if there is an aqueous softening agent and moisturizing substances.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the child is on its side, you can make it lie flat, and administer what we have said about live infants;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	And if we cannot manage it, then divide the patient into parts, and do not leave anything of the remainder.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, it moves towards that which we said about apertures where abscesses emerge in the marital area;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	And if there is a draining of blood, it should be immersed in water and restrained, and he moves towards other treatments.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman who had given birth to one child in her belly, then another followed from that womb, and this other one also died.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, an abscess came out in the belly, and it swelled so much that when it opened, it started to cause severe pain.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was summoned for treatment, and I thought for a long time, and couldn't provide proper care for the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I placed a strong plaster on it, and out came a bone, and after some days another one.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was greatly amazed, for the belly does not have any bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought it was the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I want the wound, and by guiding my hands to bones, until the woman was in the best state;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	And I covered the woman long enough like this, and it would be somewhat better by the end.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	And I have included this chapter only because when the masters find an unusual thing, they should know how to provide help.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to bring back the wife to her place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	After this comes the explanation of the presser, which is included in the books;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	and at the second turning of the two shoulders of the two beings.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	Always, let the horns be more subtle than that of the restrictor, and be made of ivory or wood;
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and let the mouth of the pipe be twice as wide, and the margin of the trees must be long, and at least one and a half palms.
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and between the two limbs there should be two attachments of this same pipe, which must be firm in one and the other, at least half a palm long or slightly more.
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	And these two attachments are fixed in the mouth of the maris so that when one turns the two horns, they open.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more subtle and lighter in appearance, might be made from a cane or buckthorn stick, according to the likeness of tongs.
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	and has two shoulder joints, as you see, of the length of a palm, and two bones wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	and when you see the elbow opening to the entire tool, make the woman sit at the bed, with her hands hanging and her legs spread apart, then position both joints together in the elbow, and hold the handle of the instrument under her armpits;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then guide your hand over the entire tool in the same way as with tongs, according to the amount you see opening the mouth of the elbow, until the force makes what she desires.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	This tool consists entirely of mountains and is multiplied like its likenesses;
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	And when you have equipped them, then the work proceeds more swiftly, and they lift individuals higher because of their quantity for those.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not lose hope in the tool you have not equipped, because its necessity is not excusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the second stage is retained during childbirth, it is necessary that you instruct the mother to retain her urine, and then make her sneeze with consideration, and keep your hands on her mouth and nose;
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	And if she jumps because of this, it goes well.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If that doesn't work, take a cup and make the patient vomit or cover it, and place herbs that can open the mouth of the wife, such as poppy, rue, fennel, chamomile, clove and thyme;
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	All these herbs, or none of them, whether cooked or steeped in water on the fire;
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	Then place a reed or a small straw in the opening of the pot, and put another end into the mouth of the patient, and blow until the steam goes inside the patient;
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	Then make them sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the second one leaps quickly.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	And if she still has no power after this treatment, and it is not strong, instruct her to moisten her left hand in sesame oil or rosemary oil, and then use the hand as nature intended, seeking out a second one;
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	And when she finds it, grasp and extend it slowly and straightly, so that the patient does not vomit during extraction;
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	But you must gently move it to the right and to the left, and then pull;
si venra et se desaerdra.	If it comes and gets relieved.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the mouth of the sore is salty and there is constriction, as we have said for the treatment of sneezing and herb vaporization;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it is not relieved by all that we have said, be careful not to overly pull during the treatment;
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	But it is necessary that the one at the mouth of the sore be tied to the woman's ovary, then anoint with a fourfold herbal ointment enema;
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	If it is applied and will cure, and will come to power;
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	However, if there is a bad smell coming from the stomach and head and reddens the skin, even when it should be curing.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	Therefore, then you need suitable fumigations for this:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	None of the old have experienced fumigation with sow's ears and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The shape of the tool with which one fumigates the woman during the retention of flowers and the afterbirth is thus:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And imagine it as a cane, and place the subtle head in the fire, and have the shoulders wide above the flame;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	And let the fumigations be over the coals, and stay until the head is exhausted, then repeat another one.
de percier lou fondement	To pierce the base
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who do not have the foundation pierced, but rather have subdued one subtle and misguided:
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	Therefore, then at the birth let it pierce that misguided element according to its nature, and do not allow it to be pricked by sharp pain, and guard against it so as not to touch it;
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then place on wet wool in wine and oil, then the application of ointment until it's clean.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it won't slip back, place or insert a tourniquet cord and leave the hands bound, and have it removed when the child desires to go into chambers.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And here comes the treatment for those sudden injuries to wounds or abscesses;
si covient coper celui soudement:	if it is necessary to cover that hot application:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	either treat with an ointment, as we have mentioned for the snail's slime.
de la fistule dou fondement	of the fistula from the foundation
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas that come from the foundation are concretion, and grow larger than those that come from below, or in the space between two parts, if it's one fistula or more;
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	and when that concretion is old, if it moves, and accumulates moisture causing white or fine yellow fluid, and always these fistulas are external;
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	And they are known by those who experience loss or windiness when a person is expelling waste, and sometimes jumping from one to another.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And for those that reach up to the bladder, and even halfway down the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	They also extend up to the knee joint, and even to the kneecap.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one can identify a fistula that occurs at the base, and not occurring there:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	And if you pierce your index finger or the base, and insert a fine needle like that of an arachnid or iron into the fistula when there is no twisting.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if there is twisting, if you insert a thin thread like that of a spider, or the hair of a horse, as long as you feel the thread or the hair on your index finger;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	And if you do not feel it, and there is no sign of decay or wind or disease anywhere nearby, as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	know that it does not pierce through;
si te haste dou curer.	if you hasten to cure it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula is passing up to the bladder or up to where urine leads, if it jumps with urine, and cannot be soldered by medicines.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it has pierced up to the knuckle, then there is a test coming up to the elbow;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	if there is no twisting and the pain is not internal, then it means that it is embedded deeply, and it does not warrant medicine or immediate ointment treatment;
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and for these Persian abscesses there is no effective remedy other than effort and the vanity of those who intervene.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In those that are neither Persian nor ancient, there is hope for healing through iron treatment, as I have experienced, and it is that the patient lies on their back with the disease in your hands;
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	And he raises the legs up to his thighs, and has his thighs inclined towards his belly;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	Then tie up an arachnid bag, or a snail if there's complexity, as long as you know where the bag comes from.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the patient feels pain in the foundation, then you should push your index finger, and if it is so that the bag has pierced.
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	And when you can feel between your index finger and the heart or flesh, then know that it is deep.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	If there's no movement, one cannot judge properly.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	We can still say that quite often we can judge well to heal some, but this happens rarely.
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	And when we assist like this, one heats up the fine cautery according to the width of the fistula, as was previously mentioned.
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	And it boils all the way inside the fistula until it escapes from under the foundation;
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	And do this two times or three, until you know that these burned-out parts are done, which resemble a bird's feather;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	Then use the moist wadding in ointment until that burned part comes out, then apply the ointment to seal and mend it.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If it's like this, then it's well.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If this is done, no other means can make it well;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	And if you push it through and does not pierce to the root which is the foundation, and between your thumb and the tent you place a thick layer of tissue or flesh, and you see the opening of the fistula under that layer until it comes into contact with the healthy tissue;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	If it's applied at the start of the fistula formation, and is held in place until the tent starts to come out, then apply the cautery afterwards, until it reaches the head of the tent.
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	And the tent will be released, and the condition will improve;
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	Then remove those hollow hairs that resemble a bird's feather, ensuring none remain.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the wound does not heal, cut between you and the wound, then apply either fire or medicinal treatment.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cauteries gather two good things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	This means, the scorching of these treated hairs, and the bleeding of blood and drying out of moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	Then treat wet tents with butter or ground things, until the pus flows out, and out comes the burnt hair in the flow.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	Then treat the wound with binding remedies consisting of hard matter, and apply them as dry medicines.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is healed, if it has truly healed and does not recur.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if the fistula comes just past halfway through the base, and is distant from the body, you should press on or inquire about its foundation.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you feel the tent [a term possibly related to a medical technique or condition], and there is II something akin to webbing, silk, or rope inside, or it's about to pierce, assuming only paths of love and hope exist, through administering one of the three ways:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	or you cauterize it as we have said, or you remove it up to the bottom, or if you can identify the tent [a term possibly related to a medical technique or condition], treat accordingly and then apply first aid;
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not overheat it, so you don't cut into the structure that holds the foundation, allowing for the eliminations to pass by its own will;
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then treat it as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	By chance if it is healed, or you remove that covering and clean it since it has been cut from the bottom, either by try or with another tool pointed.

si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	if it is easier for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And always follow this manner for the fistulas:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	And when you bend the needle in the fistula, and it is located under the foundation close to the skin above, if you take a needle that pierces the head according to this shape:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And tie two twisted threads together, and blow the tent into the fistula until it reaches to the head.

et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	and pull the head of the thread, and join both ends together, and hold one to the other, and leave it for one or two days.
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and hold it each time until the threads join these bars that are between the two, and bind them together.

Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not puncture, make an incision in all possible ways that you can, as long as it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not proper to perform such placement directly and then proceed with treatment as we have said, until the wound heals.

et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	And on the other hand no, because one doesn't join what one shouldn't join, as you see here:
des emorroydes	of lacerations
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	Illnesses occur in two ways:
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	They can occur internally, like in the resin's core, whether small or large grains are present. mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	However, those that remain outside can have little moisture, and even a bit of yellow water or a bit of blood, and they have the color of flesh;

Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	It is necessary for you to sew it up in this manner:

et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And let it grow until it becomes greasy, and when they fall off, then apply ointment treatment and other remedies, until the wounds are healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	so that drying occurs due to fire or foundation
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Many times there is the drying effect of dung in the intestines, and due to the nature's constraint, and when the disease is old and medicine no longer works.

puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat it until it is healed.
dou fremit	When the tremor
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	A worm is a small external appearance before the body, and goes all around;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And always feel the truth in it when it's cold, and you can also sense its death throes like a shiver, and it spreads throughout the body, and more so in the hands than elsewhere.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment is that you take a stick from a goose feather or a strong vulture feather and place this stick over the quivering area, until the purplish circle completely surrounds the quivering.

de la forme dou clistere	in the shape of a bladder

Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Therefore, when one applies them in the treatment of infants and those who are weak and painful, they are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The shape of the small and large blister is as follows, or how the belly is bound according to this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	And there is often distress where the belly is bound, as you see, and the bowels are pierced within.

des plaies	of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	We have spoken about the treatment of wounds in the section on wound care;
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	Or we will tell you about hand treatments and medical practices, according to their completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse depending on how they are made, and depending on where the wounds are located, and for what reason they were caused.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The causes of wounds are from the splintering of stones, and the cutting of swords and knives, or spears or bows or arrows, or similar things;
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	or those that are made according to the parts of the body, such as a wound in the neck, or on the head, or the back, or the belly, or the liver, and similar members;

Then treat the wound with medicine, and replace hard tissue for skin in its place, instructing the patient to consume hearty meats such as cooked tests and wheat, along with other similar items.

et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	And if there's an artery in the wound or vein, then without hesitation, and it cannot be stemmed by medicine, so you should clip the artery, and if you find it protruding, tie it with a thread.

de la plaie dou col	from the wound in the neck
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	This wound comes from the neck and if it is simple, there should be no difference between it and those in the head, but if a vein or an artery is cut.

de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	From the wound of a spear or a knife

s’elle est grans, de cousture;	if it is large, with stitches;
et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	and if it is small, with powder, and if there are fragments in the bone or have been removed from it, if you cleanse the wound, and if any external treatments were performed;
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	and if they have not been removed, let the wound fester, and facilitate the extractions;
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	And for other wounds on other limbs is the judgment made, just as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	regarding the protrusion of the abdomen
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	The swellings of the belly are large and medium-sized and small;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	From a major wound, sometimes the intestines rupture, or the nerves of the intestines, through which foreign substances can enter;
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans, por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	And the stitches are more troublesome; and it is not worse to have a small wound than a large one, because in the case of major injuries we do not reattach the intestines as closely, unless they are done stitch by stitch;
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes, et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres II.	Because the intestines swell whenever they feel cold; if we do not reattach them more closely, and for that reason it's better to have smaller wounds; because we must sew the intestines back in their place with care, just like with others II.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc IIII manieres:	And know that rupture of the belly occurs in four ways:
les II costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre, et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et II autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	The two common sutures occur in the belly wound, and the suture for other chest wounds is shared with other injuries;
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	Yet they are more specific to the belly suture, and I will mention each one individually and explain them.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer, et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des II manieres:	I say that when the wound is small and there's nothing of the intestine exposed, and when a matter is to be placed back, this can be done through one of the two ways:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit, ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	or due to the smallness of the wound, as we have said, or because of the swelling of the intestines from cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it's cold, heat him up in this manner:
moillie une esponge ou I mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement, ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique, et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	Moisten an sponge or add salt to water solely, or cook in boiling water with vinegar and lime and needles, and release the intestine until the internal wound is healed;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	And once this wine has been strained and made muddy to relieve swelling.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites, car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	And when you see the swelling leave, moisten the intestine with water or broth that has been cooked in salt, because through this, only little things pass through the entry.
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	And if it cannot enter, make a little incision with the tool used for extracting worms;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille, que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	And the first treatment is made muddy that the cut, which we do not have to make without great necessity or purpose;
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	And these are the instruments to split them:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	if you cut from within at the curve and not outward, and see this shape:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer, si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre, se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	And when the wound has been enlarged, and the intestines have escaped, if you can place them again according to their natural form in their proper location, then do so because this is beneficial.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre, si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	When the wound is broad, and it's in the lower belly area, you should have the patient lie on their back, and place their legs higher than their head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre, si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz, et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des II parties si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	And if it's in the lower belly region, place their head and buttocks higher than the other parts, and similarly, if the abdominal rupture is in one of the two areas, position yourself so that the affected part is higher than the other;
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	And thus, you should administer what I say in large and medium wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet, puis aies entre tes mains I ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main, et assemble les levres;	For small wounds, use what you have at hand, then take the priest's oil in your hands and smear it over the entire rupture with one hand, then bring together the lips;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures, et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie, puis laisse des le chief de la plaie I doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait I boin fil fort;	And this is the common method of suturing, and you take one or more needles according to the size of the wound's width, then leave at the edge of the wound an allowance of space, and place a needle where there will be enough strong thread.
et perce les II chiés dou cuir avec les II chiés dou siphac, qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie, et assemble les II chief dou siphac les IIII ensamble;	and pierce the two ends of the skin with the two ends of the thorn, which is inside the skin, as long as you make it pierce that part, and join the two ends of the thorn in four bundles;
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de II pars, puis assemble les II chiés de la plaie avenanment, et puis laisse I doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	then insert two strands of thread through the needle from both sides, then join the two ends of the wound together properly, and then leave an allowance of space, and place another needle;
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille, et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles, tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	then tie the thread like you did with the first needle, and continue doing this according to how many needles you need to use until all the wound is restrained;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses, car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	And use needles of medium size, between subtle and large ones, for subtle needles cut all the flesh, and overly large ones do not fit well at all.
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	because it is necessary that they be medium;
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir, k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	and it is not good to have needles sticking too far out of the flesh and skin, as they cut and open the wound before suturing;
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir, et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir, et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and then remove the needles when they are no longer needed, to prevent bruising for the patient during sleep, and cover the needle holes with bandages or cloths to keep them clean until the wound is healed;
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies, car il i soffist une aguille ou II.	and this method of stitching needles works better for small wounds, because you can use only one needle or two.
Li seconde costure si est commune, et est que tu assemble les II chiés dou cuir et les II chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait I fort fil moien;	The second stitch is common, and it consists of joining the two ends of skin and the two ends of muscle together on one needle with a strong thread in the middle;
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz IIII ensamble, si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	And when you have pierced all four ends together, you should then reset the needle at the part where you started, in the manner one sews linen;
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	and place an interval between each stitch equal to that of a small thumb;
ceste costure sevent li home, et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre, qui estoit navrez d’un coutel, et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant, et issoit des intestines bien II palmes de grant, et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	These stitches close the wound; I sewed a belly incision that a man had or had lost his intestines to due to a knife cut, and the wound was over a palm's length, with well two palms of intestines inside it, within the belly.
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit XXIIII houres fuer, et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a XV jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	I brought back the intestines until it had been 24 hours since he had them, and the wound was sewn up until 15 days, and I treated him, and he recovered.
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	And the doctor had judged that he would die, and it was a wonder;
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en I leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	And I would not treat it with ointment, for I was in a place where none could be found, nor any medicine;
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel II fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	And I would change the old cotton twice daily over the wound, and wash it with honey water until it healed.
Or vos dirai les II propres manieres de cousture:	I will tell you two proper methods for stitching:
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	Take the needle and thread it through from the outer part up to the inner side;
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille, et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	When it has pierced the right in a straight line, if it passes through the sinew or sticks or where you have threaded the needle, and you make it pierce from the inner side to the outer part again.
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz, et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	And the understanding of this stitch is that you sew it as the pelt maker does with the skin, and you leave one side of the sinew on one side, and take it from the other, until the entire seam is completed.
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement, si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les II parties ensamble naturelment, et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	The second method of sewing, as Galen properly states, is such that no one does, who unite the two parts naturally together, and apply one edge to the other edge, in this manner:
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement, et laisse les II chiés dou syfac;	Nail an awl or edge at the joint of the mirror near, and pierce only that area, and leave the two edges of the fabric;
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, as II chiés dou syfac;	Then turn the needle, and make it pierce from the outer part all the way inwards, at both edges of the fabric;
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en II autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	Then pierce both at the outer part all the way inwards up to where it's inside, with two other awls at each side of the fabric that are opposite to each other;
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	And this is the method they stitch and it is the most common one.
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent, c’on doit coudre le ventre a II aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	Galen stated this phrase, and no one attests to it, so one must suture the belly with two needles, or where there is thread in each.
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	and must one stitch with one needle from one side and the other from the opposite, like those who sew bullets;
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre, si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	and know that when the rupture is in the middle of the belly, the suture is more painful than others' bellies.
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	The judgment of the wound is like the judgments of other wounds:
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee, si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout;	and it is that when you find the fresh wound completely filled with blood, as the art has made it flow, then restore to its normal state, and the intestines, and the cut;
puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char, et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	then place on the healing powder for charcoal, and if the art has made it flow, then apply no cream that might be available until the wound heals;
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	And twist the thread, and may they缝the needle, and let them sew the skin.
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat the wound as usual, until it heals;
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel, et le remue II fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	And if you don't have medicine, place it there, intermittently until the pus begins to drain. Use old cotton, and shake it twice a day until it heals.
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	For you don't need any other medicines when dealing with simple wounds;
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz, si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset, et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	And if you suspect that the wound might affect major body parts, it's necessary to immerse the affected area in a light oil heated with heat or rose oil, and place it between the joints, covering them completely;
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient, si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	And if you feel pain or gangrene in the bowels, and this happens repeatedly, it's advisable to use black wine as an enema, and similarly, if gangrene spreads up to the intestines;
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	And pierce within it, and know that when it is the large intestine, it is easier to heal than the small ones.
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez, et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	The intestine which is called 'youth' cannot heal when it is injured, and this is due to the obstruction of blood vessels that are present there, and because of the subtlety of his entire body, and the approach of its nature towards nerves.
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	And if the pus jumps out of the wound, set it back in the same way as an intestine, while it is still fresh;
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, car il i a voinnes et arteres;	And if it is old and turned red or black, you should tie the black area, so that no blood flows out, because there are veins and arteries;
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien, et met les II chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	Then cut out what's between the tie and put the two pieces hanging down from the part under the wound up until beyond it to ease extraction when the pus discharges, and the wound will heal.
de la routure dou boueil	from the rupture of the boil
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite, si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes, por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	When the intestine is intact and the wound is small, one can attempt to restore it in some animals, for I have seen that a man was wounded or had his stomach pierced by a spear;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac, et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	And there was a wound on the right side of the stomach, it became inflamed and formed into a fistula, causing malabsorption and flatulence;
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I applied the cure according to what I knew, and didn't stop refining until it was effective, and bound up his wounds.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw them healing, I worried that the patient might be suffering in their stomach;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	But there was no harm, only improved condition, and eating and drinking took place.
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	And they told no experimenter that when there is a small wound in the intestine, it should be treated in this manner:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie, et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les II levres, si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	Take large intestines, then join the edges of the wound. And when the intestines have opened their mouths, place them against the two edges if they push their mouth upwards;
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier, puis met I autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	And then lift his head, and this is held so that it cannot be released, then another tremor follows in the same way as before, until the wound is entirely healed.
et cout la plaie.	and there is no wound left over.
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide, et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste, en teil maniere:	That is the main thing that gets into the intestine, and it causes no harm to the patient, and one can tie the intestine with a fine thread that has been cut from an animal's intestine in this manner:
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez, et puis lie au chief de cest fil I fil de lin subtil tort, puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	Take the tip of this intestine thread that has been thoroughly rubbed, and then tie it to the tip of the thread made from fine linen, twist the linen thread around the intestines, sew through the needle, stitch the intestines, and reset them in the wound;
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	And this way of stitching doesn't deviate from following the path of love and hope;
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	And if the wound is large and broad, especially when it's in one of the large intestines, so that there's no embryo or healthiness, due to subtlety.
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	from a fistula, or wherever it may be.
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule», et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	Know that any wound or abscess, when it matures, is universally called "fistula", and even when it is hair-covered and drains slowly.
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor, et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	And the fistula is along with a hard and whitish lump-like formation, where one does not feel pain, and it's also feathered like the feathers of a bird;
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	And sometimes in a clear jump, and at other times thick;
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	Sometimes small, and at other times large enough;
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char, ce n’est fuers que par une des VIIII causes:	And I have spoken about it in the section on wounds, that every wound that is not healed and has no pus exits through one of the nine causes:
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	That is to say, by the weakness of blood or bruises;
ou por sa malice;	for its wickedness;
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	because of the hardness within it, and above the lips, that does not allow hair to grow;
ou il i a trop de bowe;	because there is too much blood;
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	or the lungs are putrid, and the matter has bad quality;
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	or the medicine is not good in the treatment;
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	or because the corruption happens like a plague;
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	or due to the property in the area being late for digestion, and delayed healing, and escaping naturally;
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	or there are veins or bones;
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	and I have already shown all these causes, and the signs, and the remedies using medicine in this section.
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	So it is necessary for me to tell you about the treatment of a fistula which is done through manual work.
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	Know that fistulas occur in all limbs of the body;
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners, ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes, ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	for there are fistulas that come from the large veins, and arteries, and nerves, or at the heart, or in the intestines, or in the bladder, or on any of the ribs, or in the spinal column, or on any joint of the hands or feet;
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	and if it affects the principal property of the limb, and manifests itself accordingly.
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	And all fistulas that occur in this manner cause difficulty with healing and there is nothing else except for dirt and lack of knowledge;
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure, et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	And if there is no fistula that does not reach what I have said, and you are familiar with the cure, then find out about it. If the fistula is straight, take an araneous or iron tent, place it where the fistula is, and perform the procedure.
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc, car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	And if the fistula is twisted, seek with a delicate attempt to pierce, for the needles bend and move within the twist.
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes, si la clisterize par l’un des pertus, car la moistors si cort d’un pertus a autre, et la mundifie;	And if the fistula has twisted sides and you cannot properly search for it with attempts, insert a catheter through one of the twists, because moisture will flow from one twist to another, and clean;
puis la quier saigement a ton pooir, que tu conoisses s’il i a os ou nerf, et est chevee em parfont, et demande bien au malaide de la dolor qu’il sent au presser de ta main, et le leu ou il la sent;	Then guide your hand carefully as you can, to determine if there is bone or nerve and how it feels beneath the skin. Ask the patient precisely where they feel pain when pressed by your hand, and determine the location.
et quant tu savras vraiement le leu ou elle est, et s’elle est loing de jointure, ou de nerf, ou d’artere ou de voine, ou en aucuns des leus que je t’ai dit, si la cope selonc ceu que je t’ai dit, et oste fuer la fautreure et les chars corrumpues que sont dedens;	And when you truly know its location and if it is far from a joint, or nerve, or artery or vein, or any of the locations I mentioned, follow as I instructed, remove the bone and eliminate the putrefying substances that are inside.
et puis la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee, et se li fistule est bien parfonde de droit endroit, si covient que tu copes em parfont, tant com tu pues, puis i met tentes moillies en medicine ague, et les boute jusc’au chief de la fistule, tant que li medicine corrode la superfluiteit qui est demoree au fons;	And then the treatment until it is healed, and if a fistula exists, it must be well cut in the proper location, so you should press hard with your fingers, as much as possible, then I place moistened cloths in an ointment, and apply them up to the tip of the fistula, while the medicine eats away at the excess that has remained at the bottom;
et puis i met oignemens enjanrans sainne char, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And then I place salve on healthy tissue until it heals.
et s’il n’est sanez par ceu, si le cauterize si com nos avons dit, et se li os est corrompus de la fistule, si le cope.	And if it doesn't heal with this method, then apply the cautery as we have described, and if the bone is rotted by the fistula, then press on it.
Se voinne ou ners ne te greve ou membres principelz, si com nos avons dit;	If the vein or major limbs are involved, as we have said;
et se li os est descovers, et il i a corruption et noiror, si lou reis tant que li corruption soit toute ostee, puis le cure de choses enjanrans char tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if the bone is exposed, and there's decay and blackness, then you should scrape it until all decay has been removed, then treat with salve on healthy tissue until it heals.
et s’il n’est sanez, et rent bowe si com devant, saiches que tu n’es mie alez jusc’a font:	And if it is not healed, and you return it as before, know that you are not yet finished until the end.
si descuevre et quier tant que tu soies au fons, et oste toute la corruption, puis restore le leu;	If you uncover and seek as far down as possible, and remove all the decay, then properly return it to its place;
et s’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	And if it is so healed, that's well done.
Se ceu non, saiches que la corruption est trop en parfont, que tu n’i pues avenir;	If not, know that the decay has penetrated too far, and you cannot rectify it;
si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier a nature;	if there is no other way but to leave it to natural processes;
et s’il i a i petit os corrumput, et tu le pues traire as tenailles, si l’estrai a I estrument covenauble a ceu, et s’il i a maint os, si les trai trestoz, ne n’en laissier nes un;	And if there is a small decayed bone, and you can pull it out with tongs, if you remove it using an appropriate tool; and if there are many bones, then remove them all, do not leave any;
et se li moistor te fait contraire, et il n’i a error ne paour, si cope et moistor et char, et delivre les os.	And if moisture causes it against your will, with no mistake or fear, deal with the moisture, muscle and flesh, and free the bones.
Et se tu ne les pues oster a une houre, si met sus la plaie chose enjanrant porriture, et laisse tant que li leus soit porris entor les os, et adonc si avront plus legierement les os;	And if you cannot remove them in one hour, put on the wound a substance that promotes gangrene, and let it be until the flesh has rotted inside the bones, then they will have their bones easier.
et se c’est uns grans os, si com de jambe ou de cuisse, si reis tant soulement la corruption tant que li noiror soit toute ostee, puis restoure la plaie;	And if it is a large bone, such as from the leg or thigh, you only need to let the putrefaction proceed until all of its blackness becomes bone dust, then restore the wound.
et s’il en i a grant partie dou corrumput, et vient jusc’a mole de l’os;	And if there is a large part due to putrefaction, and it reaches up to bone dust;
si le covient soier et coper tout jusc’a la corruption, et puis le cure tant qu’il soit soudez;	And if necessary, he should treat all the way until the putrefaction stops, and then treat it as long as it is healing;
et je te dirai d’une fistule qui avint I home en sa jambe, si que tu i preignes exemple et aide en ton ovraige.	And I will tell you of a fistula that occurred in his leg, so that you may take an example and aid yourself in your work.
Il fut I jovencelz entor XXX ans, qui ot une dolor en sa jambe d’une cause que vint dedens le cors, tant que les matieres vinrent a la jambe, et fut enflee d’un gros aposteme, et n’ot point de cause defuer por ovrir;	He was a young man around thirty years old, who had pain in his leg due to something that came from within the body, until the materials reached the leg, and then there appeared a large abscess, and no external reason existed for opening it;
mais li mire par lor folie ovrerent tant sus que li apostemes ovri, et en corroient mout de matieres, et devint fistule, et i vint mout de pertus que tuit gitoient bowe et moistor dou cors;	but the physician by their foolishness opened so much that in relation to the abscesses opening, they consumed a great amount of material, and it became a fistula, and it caused immense loss that all lamented the wasting and moisture within the body;
et maint mire i mirent cure entor II ans, et n’i ot nul saige en l’art de mains, tant que je i fui apelez, et vi sa jambe et les medicines dont on le curoit, et ceu que corroit par les pertus a grant cors;	And many physicians tried to treat it for two years, and there was no wise man in the art of healing hands until I was called, and I saw his leg and the medicines used to cure him, and what consumed through the losses was with great concern within the body;
et devenoit rouges li cors dou jouvenceil, et avoit color citrine.	And became red the bodies of the young, and had a yellowish hue.
Je boutai une tente en l’un de ces pertus, et puis cerchai toz les pertus, et trovai que li uns venoit encontre l’autre de toutes les parties de la jambe.	I pitched a tent on one of these bumps, and then searched all the bumps, finding that some were coming against each other from every part of the leg.
Je me hastai donques, et copai en l’un des pertus tant que je descovri une partie de l’os, et le trovai corrumput et perciet, et venoit li corruption jusc’a l’os dedens;	So I quickly proceeded, and searched in one of the sections until I discovered a part of the bone, and found it corrupted and perforated, and the decay extended up to the inner bone;
je soiai ceu qui m’aparissoit de l’os corrumput, et cuidai qu’il n’i eust autre corruption, fuer que celi que je ostai;	It was clear to me what appeared from the corrupted bone, and I thought there wasn't any other decay, just that which I had uncovered;
et comensai a restourer la plaie de medicines sodans par lonc tens, et ne pot souder;	And I began to heal the wound with medicine for a long time, and was unable to stitch it;
et puis rencomensai, et descovri l’os si com devant, et trovai la corruption continuee en l’os, et la soiai, et puis l’ostai, et me penai de souder le leu;	And then I restarted, and discovered the bone as before, and found the decay continuing within the bone, and I removed it, and I was concerned to stitch the wound;
mais je ne pou tant que je copai entor une palme de l’os, et le traï fuer a tout son mole, puis le restourai de medicines;	But I can't do much until I've measured inside a palm of bone, and treat it thoroughly throughout, then return it with medicine;
et il fut sanez et soudez hastanment, et ne covint plus rencomencier l’ovraige fors por la foibleté dou malaide, qui ne pooit soffrir, et por la paour de mort que je avoie de lui.	And it was quickly cured and strengthened, and there was no need to restart the work except due to the weakness caused by illness, which could not endure, and because of my fear of death that I had for him.
Car por l’evacuation sanglotoit sovent, mais il fut sanez entierement, et nasquit en leu de l’os une char dure, et fut de bone disposition et n’ot point de nuisement ne de contraire dou tout en tout, ne a l’aleir ne a venir.	For in the draining of blood there is often much, but it was entirely clean, and from the place where the bone used to be emerged a hard flesh, and it had good properties and did not cause any harm or opposition at all everywhere, neither inward nor outward.
Et se li os est brisiez en aucun leu dou cors, si le covient soier en ceste maniere:	And if the bone is broken in any part of the body, it should be treated in this manner:
pren I liien, et l’estrain au chief de l’os qui apert, et comande aucun k’il l’estende en haut;	Take hold of it, and stretch to the tip of the bone that is exposed, and command that he extend it upwards;
et met I autre lien de lainne plus gros dou premier liien, et le lie sus la char qui est desor l’os, et estent le chief, si que tu traies la char corrumpue au desoz, et descuevre la char sus le leu ou tu vues soier, que li soie ne blece la char;	and make another rope of thicker wool than the first one, and bind it above the flesh that is inside the bone, and pull the tip upwards, so that you draw the rotten flesh outwards, and reveal the flesh on the part where you need to see, ensuring the bone doesn't hurt the flesh;
et met I tison ou une tauble desoz l’os por mues coper la char corrumpue;	And insert a charcoal or a board under the bone to cleanse the putrid flesh;
et covient tant soier com on puet veoir et sentir la corruption, et soier ancor autre fois.	And one must be as thorough as possible when observing and feeling the corruption, and do it again if necessary.
Et se li os est corrumpus, et n’apert mie, et li corruptions est en mileu ou en une partie, si descuevre la char toute;	And if the bone is putrid and does not open, or corruption is within or in a part of it, then remove all the flesh;
puis met I tison desoz, et puis soie des l’une partie a l’autre la corruption, et soit li soieure dou lonc de la corruption I poc, si com nos avons dit;	Then place charcoal there, and then cover the corruption from one part to another, and let the covering be long enough over any point of corruption, as we have said;
et se li corruptions est en la jointure, si cope la jointure corrumpue, et soie l’os ou elle contient de l’autre part;	And if the corruption is in the joint, then cut out the putrid joint and cover the bone from the other side;
et se li corruptions est en la continuation des II jointes, si n’i a autre angien que dou coper;	And if the corruption is in the continuation of two joints, then there's no other way but to cut it out;
et se li corruptions est ou poignil de la main, ou ou poignil dou piet, si est mout fort celle chose, mais toutevoie il covient que tu enquieres celle corrosion, coment elle t’apert;	And if the corruption is in or on the hand, or close to the foot, it is very strong but you must inquire about this corrosion, how it has appeared;
et la mundifie en toutes les manieres que tu pues, mais que li voine ou li nerf ne te faicent contraire;	and cleanse in all ways that you can, but make sure that the vein or nerve does not hinder you;
et saiches que li incisoire et les soies por coper ces os sont maintes, selonc l’assise des os et l’aparance d’ous, et lor grossece et lor subtiliteit, et lor grandor et lor petitece, et lor duresce;	know that the incisors and the grooves for cutting bones are numerous, depending on the arrangement of the bones and their appearance, as well as their size and fineness, their strength and their smallness.
et por ceu covient il apareillier a chescune semblance d’ovraige son estrument;	and for each form of work, it is necessary to have the appropriate tool.
et saiches que l’uevre te moustrera l’estrument dont tu avras mestier, selonc la conissance de cest art, et le tesmoignaige des manieres des maladies;	and know that the work will show you the tool you need for your task, according to knowledge of this art, and the testimony of how diseases are, in terms of their presentation and symptoms.
si porpense l’estrument dont tu as mestier selonc ceu qu’il le covient.	If you intend to use the tool required according to what is necessary.
dou feu	with fire
Li chiés porrissent ou par cause dedens, ou par cause defuer;	The shoulder joints may be dislocated due to internal causes, or due to external ones;
et quant tu avras medicinee celle corrosion par la cure des medicines, et il ne profitent mie, si covient coper celui membre jusques au leu ou li corrosion vient, si que li malaides eschaipe par ceu de la mort, ou par la malice, qui est plus grans, de la defaute dou membre;	And when you have treated that corrosion by using medicines and if it doesn't benefit, if it should cut off that member until the point where the corrosion comes from, so that the sick might escape through this cause of death or because of malice, which is greater than the fault in the member;
et li signes si est que li membres devient noir, si qu’il semble qu’il soit ars dou feu, et porrist aprés la noiror, pues va celle corrosions de membre em membre, et prent par tout le cors;	And the signs are that the member becomes black, as if it were burned by fire, and after the blackness comes this corrosion from limb to limb, and takes over all the body;
si te haste dou coper, et se c’est par la percussion d’aucunes venimouses bestes, si com scorpion de mer et wivre et semblans, se li corrosion est au chief dou doi, si le cope, et ne li doner mie espaice de venir jusc’a la main.	If you need to cut it off, and if it's due to the impact of some venomous beasts, such as sea scorpions and snakes, etc., when the corrosion is on the head of two, if you cut it and don't give it any space until the hand.
Et s’elle vient jusc’a la main, si la cope a la jointe, si que la corrosion ne viegne jusc’a bras;	And if it reaches up to the wrist, if you pinch at the joint, so that the poison does not spread up to the elbow;
et s’elle vient au bras, si le cope au coute;	And if it comes to the arm, if you grip the sword;
et s’elle passe le coute, c’est li mors, et n’i vaut amenistremens fuers que li quantitez de sa vertut;	And when it passes the sword, that is death, and only its potency can be excused that it could not have been avoided;
et tot ensi fai quant li corrosion vient ou piet:	and do exactly this when the poison comes or touches anything:
s’elle vient en la premiere jointe, si la cope aprés l’autre jointe;	And if it comes in the first joint, if you pinch after another joint;
et s’elle vient ou piet, si cope tout le piet;	And when it comes or touches anything, if you grip all of it;
et s’elle monte en la jambe, si cope a la jointure dou genoil;	And when it ascends to the leg, if you pinch at the knee joint;
et s’elle vient desus le genoil, si n’i a autre engien que dou lassier le malaide a mort;	And if it comes above the knee, there is no other way than to let the patient die;
et li maniere dou coper ou dou soier le membre si est que tu le lie desus et desoz, et estende uns menistres l’un des liiens aval, et uns autres ministres l’autre liien amont, et tu dessevre la char qui est entre les II liiens a I spatumile large, tant que li os soit descovers;	And the way to cover or sew the limb is as follows: you tie it up both above and below, and stretch one surgeon's hand on the lower side of the two threads, and another surgeon on the other thread uphill. You cut the flesh between the two threads with a wide scalpel until the bone is exposed;
puis le cope ou soie, et met de chescune part I drapeil de lin, si que li soie ne touche le leu sain, et viegne au malaide autre lesion et aposteme chaus.	Then sew or cover it, and place one piece of linen from each side, so that the sewing does not touch the healthy tissue, but moves away from other injury and abscess on the patient.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient quant tu oevres, si cauterize le leu hastanment, ou tu met sus aucunes poudres restraignans;	And when blood drainage occurs while you're working, quickly apply a cautery to the wound or place some constraining powders;
puis revien a ta medicine tant qu’elle soit acomplie, puis lie le membre navreit d’un liien covenauble, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then return to your medicine until it is completed, then bind the sore limb with an acceptable bandage, and treat it as long as it remains healthy.
et je te conterai k’il avint a I home en som piet:	and I will tell you what happened at my house in the garden:
il li avint une noiror qui sembloit arsure de feu, et celle corrosion vint premier en son doi dou piet, tant qu’elle porprist tout le piet;	He was struck by a darkness that seemed like the flame's corruption, and this devastation first attacked his garden in the south, spreading until it consumed all of it;
et quant li hons vit la corrosion, si se hasta de coper le piet, et fut sanez;	And when the owner saw the corruption, he rushed to cover his garden, and was saved;
et lonc tens aprés li revint li corrosion ou doi de la main, et il vint a moi, et je li mis sus choses repercussives aprés la mundification dou cors, et ne pot cesser li corrosions;	And later on, the corruption came back to his right hand side, and it reached me, and I treated him with counteractions after cleansing the body, yet could not stop the corrosion;
et il vot que je li copasse la main, et je ne vou, que je avoie esperance de repercuter la matiere;	And he insisted that I touch his hand, but I refused, hoping to counteract the substance;
