Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	And when the dislocation is behind, if the patient lies, as we have said in those with elasticity, and stretches the ligament properly on the affected leg, and also on the waist;
puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	Then place two prongs, one on the head and the other at the waist, then insert the prong between the goose's legs in the shape of a dislocation;
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	And plant wet cloths inside to prevent the patient from blistering, then extend each minister towards him, and place them evenly on their hand for the dislocation.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	If it returns, that's good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	If it doesn't, place on .ie., the table, and press on it like we said in glibosity, and let the patient lie on the healthy side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;	And when there is a dislocation present, it is necessary to extend the diseased leg quickly, and according to what I have said;
et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	and place the patient's limb so that it is over the diseased ankle, then press with one hand, and extend it backwards towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;	And if the dislocation is at the back, it does not need to extend the limb downwards or lift off the ground, but rather should be placed as if the hip was dislocated backwards as we have described about lying on both hips;
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	and under its back, and the limb should be extended as we have said previously, and one must press on the joint at the table;
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;	and it will be correct when the diseased leg extends its legs, and they will be equal;
adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	Therefore adjust the hips, and apply the plaster, and hold it with a bandage, so that the hip does not move;
et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;	and let it rest for three days or four, then release it, and apply the plaster on top;
et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;	and if you see that they are even, hold them in place as before, and let it rest for three days;
puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	then release it, and allow him to move gently, until the limb is strengthened.
de la dislocation dou genoil	Of the dislocation of the shoulder
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	The knees are dislocated according to three ways:
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	that is to say, inside and outside, and behind;
et ne desalue point devant.	and do not dislocate in front.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	And the signs for this are that you instruct the patient to bend their leg at their hip. If they cannot bend it towards their hip, know that they are dislocated;
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	And for the restoration of all this, you should make the patient lie straight, and extend their leg if they can, and place your back against their buttocks, and set their foot on your feet;
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment;	Then take their knee with your hands, and pull it between your fingers, then bend the two sides of the knee to form.
et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	And another helper extends their foot, until the knee returns to its place, and the signs are that they bend their leg lightly towards their thigh.
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;	And place the plaster, and allow the leg to rest against its thigh, and keep them together tightly for three or four days, then release.
et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And do not move the injured limbs until the members are reinforced.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the limb is not in place, apply strong extension, as we have said about treating the hip, until it becomes stable.
de la dislocation dou talon	On the dislocation of the heel
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heels are never perfectly reduced or completely dislocated, both inside and outside.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	And the signs so are that the ankle is swollen, and moves forward to the part where it has been dislocated.
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	The readjustment must be quick, and when it's only slightly out of place, we should gently stretch his hands towards it.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	And when it's dislocated almost completely, you should have the patient sit straight, and guide his left hand down by the leg, above the ankle;
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	Then pull his foot towards you with your right hand, and then twice with your left hand, then extend it upwards, and firmly keep the foot up.
et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	Do this twice as we have said, by squeezing and pulling on the foot;
s’elle revient, c’est bien;	If it returns, that's good;
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	If this does not work, then restart the operation, for it is remediable.
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	And if it cannot return this way, then have the patient sit up on their bed with their back touching the ground, and bury his penis between his thighs in the earth, and firmly plant it into the soil between his legs, and tie cloths around him, so as not to bruise the penis;
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	Then scrape the soles of his feet with ministers (which likely means tools or instruments), and others spread his legs out to his hands or knees, so he ties them around his neck on his chest;
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	Then spread each minister (presumably meaning instruments) equally, and place the penis between his thighs to hold it when one extends.
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	Then place the mirrors equally to reset the dislocated shoulder at his hands, and others use ministers (tools) to scrape the healthy leg above the wound, and the dislocation will return quickly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	And when it is at the correct point, then apply the plaster and bind closely above, keep it steady and firm, tie down the foot, and guard the nerves that are located under the ankle from behind, ensuring they are not too tightly bound.
puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	Then leave it for two or three days, and if the bandage becomes loose, due to the firmness;
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	Then release it on the third day or fourth, and guide the patient to move for three days;
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And if he goes beyond this period, it's not safe that he will still dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if abscesses are pressing on him and it comes to this, you must soothe him, as we have said elsewhere, until he feels better.
des dois	Of the fire cautery, command the patient to let the hairs grow long and even; and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the arms are dislocated, if they need to be properly stretched as part of their work, it is a simple matter.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	And if the dislocation is in neither the neck nor leg bone, it's necessary to have the patient lie completely flat or on a table straight up and down, and place your foot where the joints are open. Then press with your foot firmly until it returns;
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	And when they are even, and there is nothing open, you place under the foot of the patient a table with two shoulder rests. Then adjust them firmly, and leave them for three days, then release.
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And make them rest until they are healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	regarding wound care and dislocations together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When there is a wound with the dislocation and one seeks to restore it, many times it happens that the patient dies:
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	if you are not cautious in the treatment, if you do not know the art and have not practiced it for a long time, or if you are not compassionate and merciful and delaying, then do not be reckless;
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	and start with calming things like abscess removal, and leave the patient in the hands of God, if you do not see hope for their recovery;
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	And when you see hope, immediately reset the limb back to its place, so that pus and wound can heal.
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	And when the limb is back in place, administer treatments that soothe the pus and wound. Care for the wound, as it requires, with dried ointments;
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	And if there is fracture along with the dislocation, and small bone fragments, set them back into place, and do as we have instructed for simple diseases;
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	And guard against entering paths of fear, as I have said, for you must act according to your Creator's will, and by the knowledge with which you arm yourself and protect your body.
